# Plan 172.1 — Unified type engine

**Статус:** 📋 proposed 2026-06-19
**Umbrella:** [Plan 172 — Переработка компилятора: типовая система](172-compiler-rework.md).
**D-блок:** предв. **D312** (финал при impl; D311=172.2, D310=172.3)
**Ветка:** TBD (per-phase)
**Приоритет:** P1 (архитектурный долг ядра; soundness).
**Конвенции:** реализует [`compiler-conventions.md`](../compiler-conventions.md) §0 (единый источник
истины), §1 (где живут проверки), §2 (никакого хардкода).
**Шаги:** [Plan 172.2](172.2-method-arg-type-checking.md) (method-arg type-checking) —
первый конкретный шаг (часть U.1-U.3 на узком кейсе).

---

## 1. Цель

Свести типовую систему Nova из **четырёх независимых движков над разными представлениями** к
**одному** семантическому проходу, который строит **типизированный IR**; codegen этот IR
**потребляет** (только лоуэрит), C-компилятор **никогда не ловит ошибку типов**.

Это прямая реализация [`compiler-conventions.md`](../compiler-conventions.md) §0: «типы резолвятся
ровно один раз — в чекере; codegen ему доверяет; C никогда не должен ловить ошибку типов».

## 2. Мотивация — фрагментация «как есть»

Полная карта (3-агентный аудит 2026-06-19) — в [Plan 172.2 §8](172.2-method-arg-type-checking.md).
Кратко, **четыре** независимых движка типов:

1. **Checker** (`types/mod.rs`) — `Ty`/`TyCat`/`TypeRef`, best-effort inference, **частичный**
   single-overload резолв; знает stdlib через **хардкоженный** `builtins: HashSet` (:11497).
2. **Codegen** (`emit_c.rs`) — типы как C-строки, `infer_expr_c_type` (:35718, ~1900 строк
   re-derive), **настоящий** резолв перегрузок (`resolve_overload` :11140), знает stdlib через
   `ExternalRegistry` (parsed из `.nv`, :634).
3. **Const-fn pipeline** (`const_fn_closure.rs`/`const_fn_trampoline.rs`) — **третий** TypeRef
   unification/substitution + свой sig-registry.
4. **Sum-schema** (`codegen/sum_schema_registry.rs`) — layout sum-типов «параллельно» legacy
   `sum_schemas`.

**Следствия (то, что нас и привело сюда):**

- **Soundness-дыры между слоями.** Generics ловятся (raw-`TypeRef`-сравнение), скаляры — отдельной
  веткой, method-args — вообще в codegen, scalar-narrowing в method-arg — **никем**.
- **Рваная диагностика.** Часть ошибок — чистые Nova-ошибки (чекер), часть — codegen-ошибки
  (`no matching overload`), часть — уродливые `CC-FAIL` (категория str↔int).
- **Дублирование/дрейф.** Inference выражения — дважды; type→C-mapping — трижды (`simple_type_ref_to_c`
  **уже дрейфил**: u32 отсутствовал → `Vec[u32]` мис-манглился); метод-таблицы — ×4; знание stdlib —
  **дважды** (худшая поверхность: checker `builtins` ↔ codegen `ExternalRegistry`).

## 3. Целевая архитектура

```
parse → [SEMANTIC ANALYSIS: один движок] → типизированный IR → codegen (лоуэринг) → C
```

- Один резолвер/инференсер: тип каждого выражения и выбранный callee каждого вызова (перегрузки/
  методы/builtin — по типам) вычисляются **один раз**.
- Типизированный IR — единственный источник истины: каждое выражение аннотировано типом, каждый
  вызов — выбранным callee + моно-substitution.
- Один реестр методов/сигнатур/stdlib (включая builtin — из `.nv`, §2), читаемый обоими слоями.
- Codegen — только лоуэринг: читает IR, не выводит/не резолвит типы заново.
- C не ловит ошибки типов; все классы (`no matching overload`, D124, `E_IMPLICIT_NARROWING`) —
  диагностики **чекера**.

## 4. Атомарная декомпозиция (U.1.1 … U.7.3)

36 атомарных задач: каждая **независимо реализуема, коммитируема и проверяема**. Порядок — по `deps`.
**ОБЯЗАТЕЛЬНЫЙ критерий приёмки КАЖДОЙ задачи** (сверх указанного в самой задаче):

1. **Соответствие [`docs/compiler-conventions.md`](../compiler-conventions.md)** (§0 единый источник истины, §1 проверки в чекере, §2 никакого хардкода).
2. **Без упрощений (как для прода)** — никаких заглушек; неизбежное упрощение → маркер `[M-172.1-*]` + backlog, не молча.
3. **Pos + neg тесты через релизный `nova`** (см. [`docs/test-conventions.md`](../test-conventions.md)); neg — `EXPECT_COMPILE_ERROR`.
4. **0 регрессий против чистого бинаря** (чистый baseline БЕЗ `git stash` — temp-worktree/commit-reset/patch-checkout, §7 conventions) на полном сэмпле; blast-radius измерен ДО коммита.
5. Обновлены spec/D/Q/docs; коммит на задачу.

### U.1 — Единое знание stdlib (ПЕРЕРАБОТАНО: uniform-пакет-резолв, std не особый)

> **Переформулировка (2026-06-19).** Исходная U.1 «дать чекеру `ExternalRegistry`» **отвергнута**: `ExternalRegistry::load_builtins` сам хардкодит список std-файлов (`include_str!`), и её экспонирование благословило бы анти-паттерн (conventions §2). Корень: prelude **уже** импортируется обычным import-путём; std — это **путь** `stdlib_dir`, не inline-список; единственное дублирование — `load_builtins()` парсит std-файлы **отдельно** в codegen параллельно уже-инлайненному модулю. Keystone — **U.1.3**: удалить отдельный парс, построить ОДИН реестр из import-resolved модуля и отдать его и чекеру, и codegen.
>
> **Целевая модель.** CONCRETE TARGET UNIFORM-PACKAGE MODEL (verified against the actual code, not the audit's framing).  Crucial finding that reframes U.1: the uniform mechanism the principle demands ALREADY EXISTS for the prelude and std — and ExternalRegistry::load_builtins is the ONE redundant copy on top of it. Specifically: - std is already a search-path-located folder: `stdlib_dir = repo.join("std")` (nova-cli/src/main.rs:1109; threaded as `stdlib_dir: &Path` through every pipeline). It is NOT yet *configurable*, but it is already a path, not an include_str! list, for the IMPORT side. - prelude is already implicitly-imported via the NORMAL import path: imports.rs:174-189 injects `import std.prelude` (resolved as `stdlib_dir/prelude.nv`) into the entry module unless `#no_prelude`; #prelude(a,b) selects `std/prelude/<name>.nv`. resolve_module_paths(imports.rs:2144) maps a dotted module path to physical .nv files under entry_dir/repo/stdlib_dir/dep_root by ONE mechanism for user, std and deps. So criterion (2) of the principle is already met by the import resolver; the checker and codegen both consume the resulting INLINED module. - The duplication is exactly ONE thing: ExternalRegistry::load_builtins() (external_registry.rs:110-132) — a hardcoded `include_str!` array of 10 std files (string_builder/write_buffer/read_buffer/char/sync/raw_mem/ffi.cstr/net.addr/net.tcp/net.udp), parsed SEPARATELY in codegen (emit_c.rs:1335) PARALLEL to the already-inlined prelude module that codegen also receives. This is the "separate std parse in codegen" + "hardcoded std file list" the principle bans. The checker never sees it at all (its stdlib NAME knowledge is the hardcoded `builtins: HashSet`, types/mod.rs:11681). - `if name=="gc"/"bench"/"fibers"/"runtime"` (emit_c.rs:24649/24699/24727/24749) and is_intrinsic_namespace (types/mod.rs:8706 ↔ emit_c.rs:23338) are a DIFFERENT class: these lower to C runtime calls (nova_gc_collect() etc.). The .nv files (std/runtime/gc.nv etc.) are signature-only `extern "nova" fn gc.heap_size()` — genuine COMPILER INTRINSICS, not .nv-bodied. gc.nv:47-54 literally documents the hand-sync requirement. These cannot be "resolved away"; they need a declared-intrinsic mechanism, not deletion.  TARGET MECHANISM (how each principle clause is concretely met): (A) std = just-another-package via configurable search-path. Replace the hardcoded `repo.join("std")` (main.rs:1109, and the duplicate `repo.join("std")` at main.rs:1436/1546, bench/field_cache) with a resolved `StdSearchPath` that comes from: CLI `--std-path` > env `NOVA_STD_PATH` > `nova.toml [package] std` (manifest.rs) > default `repo/std`. "WHERE to find std" becomes config (allowed by §2 boundary); "WHAT is in std" (file names/signatures) stays in the folder, never in Rust. No behavior change at the default; the include_str! list is what gets deleted. (B) prelude = implicitly-imported packages via the normal import path. KEEP imports.rs:174-189 exactly as the mechanism (it already is the normal import path). The only change: source the prelude module path(s) from the same StdSearchPath, and make the set of implicitly-imported packages (currently just `std.prelude`) a named, documented set rather than a literal — but resolution stays the existing import resolver. (C) ONE resolution feeds both checker and codegen. The single resolution is the ALREADY-INLINED module (parse → resolve_imports_inline merges std/prelude/dep items into module.items). Build ONE registry from THAT module (ExternalRegistry::from_module already does exactly this for codegen at emit_c.rs:2157) and hand the SAME built registry to the checker. Delete load_builtins() (the separate std parse). For std namespaces used WITHOUT import (gc/fibers/runtime/bench in tests), the principled fix is: make them reachable through the import resolver as implicitly-available intrinsic packages OR via a single declared-intrinsic table built from their .nv signatures — NOT a checker-private hardcoded name set. (D) No builtins:HashSet of stdlib names. The checker's stdlib NAME knowledge comes from the inlined-module-derived registry + the import scope (peer_module_names already tracks imported namespaces). Only genuine language builtins with no .nv (primitives int..f64, true/false, Self/self, any, never) remain — the §2-sanctioned exception, renamed `language_builtins`. (E) No `if name=="gc"` duplication of KNOWLEDGE. The intrinsic LOWERING (gc.collect → nova_gc_collect()) is legitimately codegen's job and stays, BUT it must be driven by a SINGLE declared-intrinsic registry built from the .nv `extern "nova" fn` signatures (one source of truth for both: checker resolves the call's type from the signature; codegen looks up the intrinsic c-lowering by (namespace,method) key). The two is_intrinsic_namespace lists collapse to one shared const. This is the genuine "no parallel stdlib registry" fix and is the bridge between U.1 and U.2.5/U.6.  NET: the target is not "expose ExternalRegistry to the checker" (which would bless the hardcoded file list). It is "delete the hardcoded file list; build ONE registry from the already-inlined std module that the import resolver produces; make std-path config; hand that ONE registry to the checker; keep intrinsic lowering as a single declared-intrinsic table." A real package/search-path abstraction is MOSTLY already present (stdlib_dir + resolve_module_paths); the only NEW abstraction needed is (1) making stdlib_dir config-resolved and (2) a single declared-intrinsic registry built from .nv to replace both the checker name-hardcode and the codegen separate-parse for the namespaces that have no .nv body.

> **РЕОРГ U.1 (2026-06-20, по итогам impl-разведки U.1.3 + решения владельца).** Эксперимент
> (удалить `load_builtins`, реестр из inlined-модуля) дал два уточнения, меняющих декомпозицию.
> Соответствие [`compiler-conventions.md`](../compiler-conventions.md) §0/§1/§3.
>
> **(1) Taxonomy «что доступно без `import`» — модель Rust `std::prelude` / Go universe (§3).**
> Не «все std-пакеты неявно», а ТРИ чётких яруса:
> - **Universe / intrinsics** (нет `.nv`-тела, компилятор-примитив): примитивы `int..f64`,
>   `true/false`, `Self/self`, И intrinsics `gc/fibers/runtime/bench` (лоуэрятся в C-runtime).
>   Неявно доступны (как Go universe / Rust lang items). Это область **U.1.4** (declared-intrinsic table).
> - **Минимальный prelude** (курируемые `.nv` re-export'ы): `Option/Result/Vec/print/…` И
>   `char` → `str.from`/`str.from_codepoint` (их эмитит САМ компилятор: тест-харнесс,
>   интерполяция, `char.into()` — пользователь не может заимпортить за compiler-generated код).
>   Неявно доступны через prelude (обычный import-механизм).
> - **Библиотечные пакеты** (`.nv` с телами): `std.runtime.sync` (атомики/Mutex/…), `std.net`,
>   `std.ffi.cstr`, `std.runtime.raw_mem` — **требуют ЯВНЫЙ `import`** (как `use std::sync` в Rust /
>   `import "sync"` в Go). НЕ в prelude. Историческая доступность-без-import через `load_builtins`
>   была случайностью хардкода, не дизайном.
>
> **(2) Полное удаление `load_builtins` для БИБЛИОТЕЧНЫХ пакетов ЗАВИСИТ от U.4 (один inference).**
> Эмпирически: корпус импортит `sync` в ~0 тестов — он всегда шёл registry-only через `load_builtins`
> (только `extern`-сигнатуры), поэтому **тела** Nova-body sync-функций (`Once.try_start` и др.)
> НИКОГДА не кодогенерились. При инлайне (через `import`) всплывает латентный баг: codegen
> **повторно выводит** тип возврата метода (`infer_expr_c_type`, ~1900 строк re-derive) и врёт
> (`self.try_start_won()` объявлен `-> bool`, выводится `nova_int` → `if condition must be bool`).
> Это ровно §0/§1-анти-паттерн (codegen re-derive вместо «чекер резолвит — codegen потребляет»).
> **Чинить это патчем в codegen (добавить ещё inference) ЗАПРЕЩЕНО** (§0: «сокращать фрагментацию,
> не углублять»; §1: «правило в codegen — долг к переносу в чекер»). Корректный фикс — U.4
> (typed IR: чекер резолвит тип метода, codegen читает). Маркер `[M-172.1-U1-lib-import-needs-U4]`.
> **УТОЧНЕНО разведкой 2026-06-25 (§9-строка U.1.3b):** «один inference» оказался ДВУМЯ гэпами —
> Gap A (чекер не резолвит `self`/`@`-receiver → resolved_callees не пишется; landable сейчас, не U.4)
> + Gap B (codegen не несёт extern-return в канале; tuple/Result-возвраты = U.4.3-hazard, primitive-gate).
> Плюс typedef-redef (двойная регистрация → удаление load_builtins) + миграция (sync 146/net 10/cstr 0)
> + net-класс (net_last_error). ПОРЯДОК: звучность инлайн-пути ПЕРЕД удалением load_builtins (conventions §10).
>
> **Расщепление U.1.3 → U.1.3a / U.1.3b (новый порядок зависимостей):**
> - **U.1.3a — landable СЕЙЧАС (не требует U.4):** минимальный prelude (`char`), `CEmitter::new`
>   стартует с пустого реестра, реестр строится из import-resolved модуля (`from_module`, +
>   `receiver_types`/`type_decls`). Покрывает no-import surface (`str.from`, char-методы,
>   StringBuilder, Vec, raw_mem-транзитивно) — проверено: PASS. Это уже убирает `include_str!`
>   как ЕДИНСТВЕННЫЙ источник для prelude-поверхности.
> - **U.1.3b — GATED на U.4:** окончательное удаление `load_builtins` для библиотечных пакетов
>   (sync/net/cstr) — инлайн их Nova-body тел требует, чтобы codegen не выводил типы сам (U.4).
>   До U.4 `load_builtins` для этих пакетов **остаётся** (registry-only, чтобы не регрессировать
>   корпус), помечен `[M-172.1-U1-lib-import-needs-U4]`; это честный промежуточный шаг к §3-цели,
>   а не §0/§1-нарушение.
>
> **Следствие для U.1.5/U.1.6:** их «удаление `builtins` HashSet / `include_str!`» для
> sync/net-имён тоже наследует gate на U.4 (см. их `Deps`). U.1.1/U.1.2/U.1.3a/U.1.4 — независимы от U.4.

#### U.1.1 — Make the std search-path configurable (std becomes just-a-package located via config, not repo.join("std"))
- **Что:** Introduce a single resolution of the std package root: a `fn resolve_std_path(repo, manifest, cli_override) -> PathBuf` with precedence CLI `--std-path` > env `NOVA_STD_PATH` > `nova.toml [package].std` (or [workspace].std) > default `repo/std`. Replace EVERY hardcoded `repo.join("std")` with this resolver so std is located by config, mirroring sysroot/GOROOT. Add the `std` field to manifest parsing (manifest.rs) and the `--std-path` CLI flag. WHERE to find std = config (allowed by §2 boundary); WHAT is in it stays in the folder. Default path is byte-identical to today (repo/std) so zero behavior change.
- **Где:** nova-cli/src/main.rs:1106-1114 (resolve_paths — stdlib_dir field), :1436, :1546 (duplicate repo.join("std")); nova-cli/src/bench/field_cache_wallclock.rs:312; compiler-codegen/src/manifest.rs (add [package].std parse); new CLI flag in arg parsing near where --color is handled. Resolver lives in nova-cli (or manifest.rs as pub fn).
- **Приёмка:** POS: default build/test/check unchanged — `repo/std` resolved when no override; a fixture project with `[package] std = "./vendor/std"` (a copied std tree) compiles `import std.prelude` from the override path; `NOVA_STD_PATH=/tmp/std nova check x.nv` uses it; `--std-path` wins over env. NEG: `--std-path /nonexistent` → prelude auto-import skipped (existing imports.rs:2509 behavior) and a clear diagnostic, NOT a panic. Conforms-to-conventions: §2 boundary (where=config OK), no WHAT hardcoded; documented in a §2 note. NO simplifications: real precedence chain, no stub. 0 regressions vs clean binary on full nova test (default path identical) — stash+rebuild baseline per conventions §6.5; emitted C byte-identical at default.
- **Blast-radius:** Touches every pipeline entry that builds stdlib_dir (~5 sites) but the DEFAULT value is unchanged, so behavior is identical unless overridden. Risk surface = any site that assumed repo/std literally. Measure: grep all `join("std")`, confirm all routed through the resolver; full-sample nova test parity + emitted-C byte-diff = empty at default.
- **Deps:** none · **Risk:** Low-medium. Main risk: a missed `repo.join("std")` site keeps the old hardcode → inconsistent path under override. De-risk: exhaustive grep of `"std"` path-joins before commit; unit test asserting precedence order; default-path regression is the safety net.

#### U.1.2 — Make prelude + intrinsic namespaces a named, documented implicitly-imported set resolved via the normal import path
- **Что:** Replace the literal `vec!["std".into(),"prelude".into()]` injection (imports.rs:174-189) and the #prelude(a,b) subdir literal with a single `IMPLICIT_PACKAGES` description sourced from one place, resolved through the EXISTING import resolver from the (now config) std path. This formalizes criterion (2): 'what is available without import' = a designated set of implicitly-imported packages resolved by the normal mechanism, not an ad-hoc literal. Keep resolve_module_paths as the resolver. Do NOT yet touch the checker/codegen registries — this is purely making the implicit-import set explicit + path-sourced. The set stays exactly {std.prelude} (and the #prelude(name) → std/prelude/<name> selection) so behavior is unchanged.
- **Где:** imports.rs:167-190 (prelude auto-import block in collect_all_signatures), imports.rs:537-660 (resolve_imports_inline_ex prelude auto-import block, the authoritative one), is_prelude_self_module (manifest.rs). Introduce a `const IMPLICIT_PRELUDE_PACKAGE` / small helper consumed by both blocks (the sig-pass copy at :174 and the full-resolve copy at :537 currently duplicate the heuristic).
- **Приёмка:** POS: every existing prelude-dependent fixture still resolves Option/Result/print without import; #no_prelude still suppresses; #prelude(core) still selects std/prelude/core.nv — all via the unchanged resolver. The two duplicated prelude-injection heuristics (sig-pass :174 vs full :537) now share ONE source. NEG: a `#prelude(bogus)` still errors (bad name). Conforms-to-conventions §0 (one source for the implicit set), §2 (no hardcoded file list — resolution via import path). NO simplifications. 0 regressions vs clean binary on full nova test; emitted C byte-identical.
- **Blast-radius:** Prelude injection is on EVERY non-#no_prelude module → highest-frequency path. But the resolved package set is unchanged, so output is identical. Measure: full-sample parity + diff of which modules get prelude injected (must be identical set) + emitted-C byte-diff empty.
- **Deps:** U.1.1 · **Risk:** Medium. Risk: the two prelude-injection copies (sig-pass vs full-resolve) have a subtle divergence today; unifying could shift one. De-risk: literal-diff the two blocks first; if they differ, document which is canonical before merging; regression-guard fixture per prelude mode (default / #no_prelude / #prelude(core)).

#### U.1.3a — Minimal prelude (char) + build the registry from the inlined module for the NO-IMPORT surface (load_builtins KEPT for libraries)
- **Что:** Узкая, regression-free часть keystone (проверена экспериментом 2026-06-20). (1) `char` → prelude (`import std.runtime.char` в std/prelude.nv) — `str.from(char)`/`str.from_codepoint` эмитит сам компилятор (тест-харнесс/интерполяция/`char.into()`), пользователь не может заимпортить за compiler-generated код → обязан быть неявным (минимальный-prelude, §3 taxonomy). (2) Реестр **дополнительно** строится из import-resolved модуля: merge `from_module(module)` теперь включает не только `by_key`, но и `receiver_types` + `type_decls` (dedup by name). Покрывает no-import surface: `str.from`, char-методы, StringBuilder/WriteBuffer/ReadBuffer (prelude re-export), Vec, raw_mem (транзитивно через Vec). **`load_builtins` ОСТАЁТСЯ** для библиотечных пакетов (registry-only, нулевая регрессия) — его полное удаление — U.1.3b. char-дубль (load_builtins + inlined) безвреден: char.nv не имеет `Item::Type` → нет typedef-redef.
- **Где:** std/prelude.nv (`import std.runtime.char`, плейн, как `defaults`); emit_c.rs from_module merge (:2157 — добавить merge receiver_types + type_decls с dedup). CEmitter::new пока НЕ трогаем (load_builtins остаётся источником lib-сигнатур).
- **Приёмка:** POS: no-import surface (str.from/char/buffers/Vec/raw_mem) PASS через release nova (проверено: detect172 PASS). Byte-identical C для фикстур, не использующих char-инлайн (char externs C-кода не дают). NEG: n/a (additive). Conforms §3 (char — минимальный-prelude через обычный import-механизм). 0 регрессий против чистого бинаря.
- **Blast-radius:** Низкий — prelude инлайнит 2 char-extern (нет C-эмита); merge receiver_types/type_decls аддитивен (dedup). Default behavior не меняется для не-char кода.
- **Deps:** U.1.1, U.1.2 · **Risk:** Low-medium. Главный риск — char-дубль с load_builtins; mitigated (char без type_decls → нет redef). Проверено экспериментом.

#### U.1.3b — Delete load_builtins ENTIRELY for library packages (sync/net/cstr) — registry fully from inlined; expose to checker
> **РАЗВЕДКА 2026-06-25 (§7.1-карта, эмпирическая) переопределила задачу в УПОРЯДОЧЕННУЮ декомпозицию.**
> Решение владельца: код НЕ правим сейчас — фиксируем карту + порядок (conventions §10). Воспроизведено:
> `import std.runtime.sync` + Nova-body `try_start()` → CODEGEN-FAIL `if condition must be bool, got nova_int`.
> **ПОРЯДОК ОБЯЗАТЕЛЕН (conventions §10 «удаление registry-only снабжения до звучности инлайн-пути»):**
> сперва довести инлайн-codegen-путь до звучности (чекер резолвит ВСЕ формы вызова, codegen ничего не
> угадывает), ТОЛЬКО ПОТОМ убирать `load_builtins`. Иначе обмен рабочего shortcut на угадывающий путь.
- **Что (упорядоченные под-шаги):**
  1. **Gap A — чекер резолвит `self`/`@`-receiver instance-вызовы** (`infer_arg_ty` `types/mod.rs:11927` даёт `_=>None` для self/@ → `check_instance_overload` бейлит → `resolved_callees` не пишется = §10/§1-анти-паттерн «резолв выброшен»). Фикс ≈12 строк (зеркало SelfAccess→scope["@"] :9225), **byte-identical** (plan91_12 14/0=baseline, верифицировано в разведке; код откатан). **Landable сейчас, не гейтнут на U.4.** §1-материализуй.
  2. **Gap B — codegen потребляет return extern-методов из канала** (`fn_ret_by_span` исключает extern: ранний выход `is_external` `emit_c.rs:9402`). **Наивно (через `return_type_c`) = РЕГРЕССИЯ:** tuple/Result-возвраты (net `split`/`recv_from`) расходятся с legacy mono-tuple → `_NovaTuple_2_8` CC-FAIL (plan91_12 14/0→7/7) = U.4.3 hazard. ⇒ **primitive-gate** (как U.4.4) для немедленной части; полный (tuple) = **U.4.3** (типизированный IR). НЕ патчить codegen новой инференцией (§0/§1).
  3. **Удаление `load_builtins` для lib-пакетов** (external_registry.rs:110-132; emit_c.rs:1335 CEmitter::new → empty registry) — снимает `typedef redefinition` (двойная регистрация типов: load_builtins + инлайн-модуль; ПОДТВЕРЖДЕНО на sync `Nova_Mutex`). Реестр строится из import-resolved модуля; тот же реестр — чекеру (types/mod.rs check_module_impl :105/:787, NameResCtx).
  4. **Миграция корпуса** (lib-без-import → добавить `import`). **Объём (ИСПРАВЛЕНО, только `.nv`): sync 146 / net 10 / cstr 0 / raw_mem 3.** cstr = **0 миграции** (все уже import) → НАИМЕНЬШИЙ первый срез. raw_mem почти n/a (3; раннее «798» = `.c`-артефакты, мискаунт).
  5. **net — отдельный класс:** `undefined identifier net_last_error` (`extern "C"` helper `std/net/ffi.nv` не инлайнится транзитивно при `import std.net.*`) — резолв транзитивных net-helper'ов.
- **Где:** см. под-шаги. Gap A: `types/mod.rs:11927`. Gap B: `emit_c.rs:9402` + flip-сайт `infer_expr_c_type` (U.4.5(a)). Удаление: `external_registry.rs:110-132`, `emit_c.rs:1335`. Чекер-консьюмер: `types/mod.rs` check_module_impl.
- **Приёмка:** POS: `import std.runtime.sync`/`std.ffi.cstr` инлайнит чисто (без typedef-redef и без `if must be bool`); чекер ИМЕЕТ реестр. NEG: lib без import → чистая «undefined». 0 регрессий ПОСЛЕ миграции. Conforms §0/§1/§3/§10.
- **Blast-radius:** LARGEST в U.1: отдельный парс std + источник реестра codegen + консьюмер-чекер + миграция (~156 файлов: sync 146 + net 10).
- **Deps:** U.1.3a; **Gap A — none (landable)**; **Gap B-tuple — U.4.3**; шаги 3-5 — после 1+2. `[M-172.1-U1-lib-import-needs-U4]` (уточнён: не «весь U.4», а перечень шагов 1-5) · **Risk:** High (миграция + net-класс + Gap B-tuple). cstr-срез — Low (0 миграции).

#### U.1.4 — Single declared-intrinsic registry for gc/bench/fibers/runtime (replace BOTH the checker name-hardcode and the codegen if-name==gc knowledge source)
- **Что:** gc/bench/fibers/runtime are genuine compiler intrinsics: their .nv files (std/runtime/gc.nv:74 etc.) are signature-only `extern "nova" fn`, and codegen lowers them to C runtime calls (emit_c.rs:24649/24699/24727/24749 `if name=="gc"`...). Build a SINGLE declared-intrinsic table from those .nv signatures (parsed via the import path / std search-path, not a hardcoded list) keyed by (namespace, method) → {param/return types FROM the .nv, c-lowering tag}. The checker resolves the CALL TYPE of gc.collect() from this table's signature (no `builtins` entry needed); codegen looks up the SAME table by key to pick the c-lowering, replacing the knowledge half of `if name=="gc"` (the lowering bodies stay, but gated on a table hit, not a hardcoded name match in two places). Collapse is_intrinsic_namespace (types/mod.rs:8706) and the codegen guard (emit_c.rs:23338) to read this one table's namespace set. These namespaces are usable WITHOUT import (per gc_differential.nv) by registering them as implicitly-available intrinsic packages in the import scope (U.1.2 set) — so resolution is via the normal mechanism, not a bare-name whitelist.
- **Где:** external_registry.rs (intrinsic table built from std/runtime/{gc,fibers,runtime}.nv + std/bench.nv via the search-path); types/mod.rs is_intrinsic_namespace :8706 (read the table), the three builtins read sites :12070/:12485/:12544 (namespaces resolved via table/import-scope); emit_c.rs:23338 (guard reads table), :24649/:24699/:24727/:24749 (lowering gated on table hit). std/runtime/gc.nv:47-54 documents the hand-sync to remove.
- **Приёмка:** POS: gc.collect()/gc.heap_size() WITHOUT import (gc_differential.nv) still type-checks AND lowers to nova_gc_collect() — proven by both checker pass and byte-identical emitted C; fibers.*/bench.*/runtime.* same. The intrinsic namespace set is grep-provably ONE table (the two is_intrinsic_namespace lists reference it). NEG: gc.bogus() → checker diagnostic (method not in the intrinsic signature table), NOT a silent codegen fallthrough; a lowercase unknown namespace widget.frob() → undefined module/name. Conforms §0 (one source for intrinsic knowledge), §2 (signatures from .nv, only the c-lowering BODIES are the documented intrinsic exception with [M-172.1-U1-intrinsic-lowering]). NO simplifications. 0 regressions vs clean binary on full nova test; emitted-C byte-diff empty for all gc/bench/fibers/runtime fixtures.
- **Blast-radius:** Touches the checker's three builtins read sites AND codegen's intrinsic dispatch AND the two is_intrinsic_namespace lists — the overlap point with U.2.5. Risk: a namespace method present in the hardcoded codegen match but missing from the .nv signature file (drift) would lose its lowering. Measure: enumerate every method in the four `if name==X` blocks, confirm each has a matching `extern fn` in the .nv; reconcile drift explicitly. Detect-mode: assert table-hit set == old hardcoded-name set over the corpus.
- **Deps:** U.1.3 · **Risk:** High. The codegen match arms and the .nv signature files may have drifted (methods in one not the other); gc.nv:47 admits manual sync. De-risk: literal reconciliation of each `if name==X` arm vs its .nv file BEFORE wiring; any method only in the match (no .nv) stays a documented intrinsic with a marker; full per-fixture emitted-C byte-diff. This task is the bridge to U.2.5/U.6 — coordinate so the unified is_intrinsic_namespace lands once.

#### U.1.5 — Route the three checker name-resolution sites through the shared registry + import scope; keep only language_builtins
- **Что:** With the registry exposed (U.1.3) and intrinsic namespaces tabled (U.1.4), replace the `self.builtins.contains(...)` half at all THREE read sites with: (a) genuine language builtins (primitives int..f64/uint/size/str/char/bool/unit/any/never, true/false, Self/self) from a renamed `language_builtins` set — the §2-sanctioned exception; (b) everything else (gc/bench/fibers/runtime namespaces, fence free-fn, Fail/Detach/CancelToken types) resolved from the shared registry + intrinsic table + import scope. Factor ONE predicate `is_resolvable_stdlib_name(head)` used by all three. Behavior identical for every currently-passing input. FIRST grep-prove the resolution path of Fail/Detach/CancelToken/fence: fence is in sync.nv (already in registry); CancelToken/Fail/Detach are prelude effects/handles — confirm they reach the checker via inlined prelude/sig_table; if any resolves ONLY via this hardcode, give it a registry/type-decl home before migrating, else keep in language_builtins with a marker.
- **Где:** types/mod.rs path-head check :12070 (in_builtins), is_known :12544, is_variant_like :12485 — all replaced by the unified predicate using the U.1.3 field + U.1.4 table + peer_module_names import scope; reuse helper across all three.
- **Приёмка:** POS: gc-without-import, fibers/bench/runtime without import, CancelToken.new(), fence(), Fail[E] in an effect clause, and a pattern matching on true/false all resolve/disambiguate exactly as before. A USER type with a method named like a builtin resolves by the SAME mechanism (type-agnostic, §2). NEG: frobnicate.doStuff() (unknown lowercase namespace) → undefined module/name; bare bogusName → undefined identifier; both via EXPECT_COMPILE_ERROR. Conforms §0/§1/§2/§3 (no new silent _=>return). NO simplifications. 0 regressions vs clean binary on full nova test; corpus-wide diff of {undefined identifier, undefined module/name} diagnostics = empty delta (instrument before/after).
- **Blast-radius:** is_known (:12544) is the central undefined-identifier gate — highest of the three. is_variant_like (:12485) affects pattern binding-vs-variant. Measure: dump the set of names for which each site returns true via the builtins branch across the corpus BEFORE; assert the unified predicate yields the same set AFTER; empty diagnostic-class delta.
- **Deps:** U.1.3, U.1.4 · **Risk:** High. Fail/Detach/CancelToken may be load-bearing ONLY through this hardcode (effects have no extern fn). If so, removing them without a registry/type home breaks effect-clause resolution broadly. De-risk: grep-prove each one's non-hardcode path FIRST; migrate only when each has a home; true language-builtin effects stay in language_builtins with [M-*]. true/false MUST remain in language_builtins (pattern-semantics guard fixture).

#### U.1.6 — Delete the hardcoded stdlib names from the builtins HashSet; remove load_builtins include_str! list
- **Что:** Now that all consumers read the shared registry / intrinsic table / import scope (U.1.4-U.1.5), delete the stdlib-name entries from the `builtins` literal (types/mod.rs:11681): remove gc/bench/fibers/runtime/Fail/Detach/CancelToken/fence; retain ONLY language builtins, renamed `language_builtins` with a §2-citing doc comment. AND delete the hardcoded include_str! file array in load_builtins (external_registry.rs:112-126) now that the registry is built from the import-resolved module (U.1.3). If the `builtins` field is fully redundant, remove it. This is the soundness-bearing removal that fulfils 'no builtins:HashSet of stdlib names' and 'no hardcoded std file list'.
- **Где:** types/mod.rs builtins literal :11681-11791 (drop gc :11748/bench :11754/fibers :11759/runtime :11762/Fail :11764/Detach :11766/CancelToken :11771/fence :11787; keep primitives/literals/Self), field :11497, ctor :11849; external_registry.rs:110-132 (load_builtins file array removed/replaced by the import-resolved build).
- **Приёмка:** POS: all U.1.4/U.1.5 fixtures pass. grep proves gc/bench/fibers/runtime/Fail/Detach/CancelToken/fence absent from the checker's hardcoded set AND no include_str! std-file array remains in external_registry.rs (only genuine non-.nv exceptions, if any, documented). NEG: same neg fixtures fire identically. Conforms §0/§2 (no stdlib hardcode beyond documented language_builtins). NO simplifications. 0 regressions vs clean binary on FULL nova test (not a sample — soundness removal, §6.6); every diagnostic class diff = empty delta vs clean binary; emitted-C byte-identical.
- **Blast-radius:** The actual removal — any missed read path surfaces as undefined-identifier / wrong-pattern / lost-intrinsic here. Measure: re-grep `self.builtins`/`.builtins.contains` AND every `include_str!` of a std file immediately before; confirm the complete consumer set is migrated. Keep in its own commit for easy revert.
- **Deps:** U.1.3a, U.1.4, U.1.5 — для prelude/intrinsic-имён; **lib-имена (sync/net/cstr) GATED на U.4** (см. РЕОРГ-заметку, `[M-172.1-U1-lib-import-needs-U4]`) · **Risk:** High. A missed consumer or a std file the import path doesn't inline (used-without-import) breaks silently. De-risk: exhaustive re-grep; the U.1.3 detect-mode registry-diff must be empty; full (not sample) regression with diagnostic-class diff; separate revertable commit.

#### U.1.7 — Tests: positive + negative proving uniform-package resolution (config std-path, prelude-via-import, registry-sourced names, intrinsic table)
- **Что:** Add fixtures via release nova (C-codegen pipeline) proving the uniform model: POS — (a) gc.collect()/fibers.*/bench.*/runtime.* without import type-check AND run (intrinsic table); (b) CancelToken.new()/fence()/Fail[E] resolve; (c) a project with `[package] std = "./vendor/std"` or NOVA_STD_PATH compiles against the relocated std (config search-path); (d) a USER type with a builtin-named method resolves by the same mechanism (type-agnostic). NEG (EXPECT_COMPILE_ERROR in neg/ folder-modules) — (e) widget.frob() unknown namespace → undefined module/name; (f) bare unknown ident; (g) gc.bogus() → intrinsic method-not-found; (h) --std-path /nonexistent → graceful prelude-skip diagnostic. Add cargo unit tests: registry built from import-resolved module exposes the same keys as the old load_builtins (parity); std-path precedence order; intrinsic table namespace set == unified is_intrinsic_namespace.
- **Где:** new nova_tests/ positive folder-module + neg/ folder-module per conventions §7; cargo unit tests in external_registry.rs + the std-path resolver module; reference error codes from spec/decisions/09-tooling.md error-index; wire EXPECT_COMPILE_ERROR per test-conventions.md.
- **Приёмка:** POS fixtures compile+run green via release nova; the relocated-std fixture proves std is config-located. NEG fixtures fail with the exact pinned diagnostic codes under --compile-error. cargo unit tests pass (parity + precedence + intrinsic-set). The user-type-with-builtin-name fixture proves type-agnostic resolution (§2). Conforms-to-conventions (tests via release pipeline, neg/ folder-modules). NO simplifications. Fixtures fast enough for the default regress sample (not the out-of-band large set). 0 regressions vs clean binary (they are additive).
- **Blast-radius:** Test-only; adds fixtures to the regress sample — confirm fast compile+exec. No production change.
- **Deps:** U.1.3, U.1.4, U.1.5, U.1.6 · **Risk:** Medium. Neg fixtures may pin the wrong code if name-res ordering shifted. De-risk: run each neg fixture once to capture the actual emitted code before pinning EXPECT_COMPILE_ERROR; the relocated-std fixture needs a copied std tree — keep it minimal (just prelude.nv + one module) to stay fast.

#### U.1.8 — Docs, spec/D-block, error-index, and §2 exception record for the uniform-package model
- **Что:** Document the full cycle (§8): (1) D-block (coordinate with D312) recording that std is now a config-located package (search-path/manifest), prelude is implicitly-imported via the normal import path, ONE registry built from the import-resolved module feeds checker+codegen, the include_str! std file list is gone, and intrinsic namespaces are driven by ONE declared-intrinsic table. (2) Record the retained language_builtins AND the intrinsic c-lowering bodies as explicit §2 exceptions with markers [M-172.1-U1-language-builtins] / [M-172.1-U1-intrinsic-lowering] (what is hardcoded + why no .nv body exists). (3) Update docs/plans/172.1-unified-type-engine.md U.1 section to the reworked uniform-package framing (supersede the old 'expose ExternalRegistry' wording, which blessed the hardcoded list). (4) Update std/runtime/gc.nv:47-54 hand-sync note (now single-table-sourced). (5) Update spec/decisions/09-tooling.md error-index only if a message changed; record any byte-drift fallback in simplifications.md.
- **Где:** docs/plans/172.1-unified-type-engine.md U.1 section (the :70-138 block reworked); a D-block in spec/decisions/ (D312 coordination); docs/backlog-followups.md / simplifications.md for markers; spec/decisions/09-tooling.md error-index; std/runtime/gc.nv:47-54 note; markers in types/mod.rs (language_builtins) + external_registry.rs (intrinsic table).
- **Приёмка:** 172.1 U.1 section reflects the implemented uniform-package model (not the old framing). Retained hardcodes (language_builtins, intrinsic lowering) documented as §2 exceptions with markers present in code AND backlog. grep of types/mod.rs / external_registry.rs for stdlib names/files returns only the documented exceptions. Reviewer can trace: claim (std=config package, one registry) → code (U.1.1-U.1.6) → tests (U.1.7) → docs (this task). spec/error-index unchanged unless a message changed. Conforms §4/§8.
- **Blast-radius:** Docs-only; zero code/behavior change; zero regression risk.
- **Deps:** U.1.6, U.1.7 · **Risk:** Low. Risk: doc drift if the registry-build / byte-drift fallback decision from U.1.3 isn't captured verbatim. De-risk: record the actual U.1.3/U.1.4 outcomes (shared registry vs checker-private; intrinsic-table reconciliation) exactly as implemented.

### Ripple на U.2-U.7 (правки от переработки U.1)

> RIPPLE ON U.2-U.7 (each existing task that changes, with specifics):
> 
> U.2 (one registry) — SIGNIFICANTLY ABSORBED. The reworked U.1.3 already builds ONE registry from the import-resolved module and hands it to BOTH layers — that is a large slice of U.2's stated goal ('ONE registry consumed by both checker and codegen'). EDITS NEEDED:
> - U.2.1/U.2.2 (define+build SigRegistry): NARROW. The std/builtin source is no longer load_builtins' hardcoded list — U.2's SigRegistry::build must consume the SAME import-resolved module + U.1.3's registry, not re-introduce a separate std parse. Add an explicit dependency on U.1.3's single-registry build; the SigRegistry is the method-SIGNATURE superset built over that same module.
> - U.2.5 (unify is_intrinsic_namespace, fold MethodSig, delete resolve_overload): PARTIALLY DONE BY U.1.4. The 'collapse the two is_intrinsic_namespace lists to one' deliverable moves into U.1.4 (the intrinsic table already unifies them). U.2.5 should be edited to (a) reference U.1.4's single intrinsic table rather than re-collapsing, and (b) keep only the MethodSig-fold + dead resolve_overload removal. Mark U.2.5's intrinsic-list bullet as 'completed in U.1.4'.
> - U.2.3/U.2.4 (checker/codegen consume the registry): UNCHANGED in mechanism but now their 'builtin source' is U.1's shared registry, not load_builtins — update the WHERE notes to cite the import-resolved build.
> 
> U.3 (resolution in checker) — DEPENDENCY HARDENED, SCOPE UNCHANGED. U.3.3/U.3.5's SOFT-dep on U.1 ('checker must see builtin Vec.push/str.* signatures') is now satisfied by U.1.3 (checker has the registry) — the [M-172-builtin-recv-pending-U1] gate can be lifted once U.1.3+U.1.5 land. EDIT: change U.3.3/U.3.5 deps from 'SOFT-dep U.1' to 'HARD-dep U.1.3 (registry exposed)'. The intrinsic-namespace calls (gc.collect) that U.3 would otherwise re-handle are now resolved via U.1.4's table — U.3 need not touch them; note this so U.3 doesn't double-resolve namespace calls.
> 
> U.4 (one inference) — MINOR. U.4 assumes resolution lives in the checker (U.3). No direct change from U.1's rework EXCEPT: U.4.4's element-type/Member arms must source field/method types from U.1's single registry (already its intent). No task edits required beyond confirming the registry referenced is U.1's, not a codegen-private one.
> 
> U.5 (one representation) — NO RIPPLE. U.5 (Ty/TyCat width/sign) is orthogonal to package/std resolution. Unchanged.
> 
> U.6 (collapse dups) — REDUCED. U.6's premise that codegen has a 'separate std parse' partly evaporates: U.1.3 deletes load_builtins' separate parse. EDITS:
> - U.6 should drop any sub-task aimed at the codegen separate-std-parse (now removed in U.1.3).
> - The const-fn/sum-schema dedup (U.6.4/U.6.2) is untouched (not std-related).
> - The intrinsic-namespace dedup is now owned by U.1.4 — remove it from U.6's scope if present.
> 
> U.7 (C never catches) — NO STRUCTURAL CHANGE, slightly EASIER. Removing the hardcoded name set and unifying intrinsic resolution removes a class of 'name resolved in one layer not the other' drift that could surface as CC-FAIL. U.7's allowlist may shrink marginally. No task edits; just note U.1 contributes to the shrinking allowlist.
> 
> SUMMARY OF EDITS: U.2.5 intrinsic-list bullet → mark done-in-U.1.4; U.2.1/U.2.2 source → U.1.3 registry; U.3.3/U.3.5 → HARD-dep U.1.3, drop namespace double-resolve; U.6 → drop separate-std-parse + intrinsic-dedup sub-items (absorbed). U.5 untouched. U.4 minor (cite U.1 registry).

> **Feasibility.** FEASIBILITY + PREREQUISITE ASSESSMENT.
> 
> PREREQUISITE: A real package/search-path abstraction is MOSTLY ALREADY BUILT — this is the single most important finding and it makes the rework tractable. Concretely: (1) std is already a path (`stdlib_dir`, threaded everywhere) not an inline list for the IMPORT side; (2) `resolve_module_paths` (imports.rs:2144) already maps dotted module paths to physical .nv files under entry/repo/std/dep roots by ONE mechanism for user+std+deps; (3) prelude is already implicitly-imported via the normal import path (imports.rs:174-189). So criteria (1) and (2) of the principle are ~80% met by existing infrastructure. The ONLY genuinely NEW abstraction needed is: (a) make `stdlib_dir` config-RESOLVED instead of literal `repo.join(\"std\")` (U.1.1 — small, ~half a day, a precedence chain + manifest field + CLI flag, default unchanged); and (b) a single declared-intrinsic registry built from the gc/fibers/runtime/bench .nv signatures to replace BOTH the checker name-hardcode and the codegen if-name==gc knowledge source (U.1.4 — the genuinely novel piece). Neither is a multi-week effort.
> 
> WHY THE ORIGINAL U.1 FRAMING WAS WRONG (confirmed): 'expose ExternalRegistry to the checker' would have the checker consume load_builtins() — but load_builtins IS the hardcoded include_str! std-file list (external_registry.rs:112-126) the principle bans. Exposing it blesses the anti-pattern. The correct keystone is U.1.3: DELETE the separate std parse and build ONE registry from the import-resolved module, then share it. This is a real but bounded refactor.
> 
> REALISTIC SIZING:
> - U.1.1 (config std-path): SMALL (~0.5d). Default path identical → near-zero regression risk.
> - U.1.2 (named implicit-import set): SMALL-MEDIUM (~0.5-1d). Unifies two duplicated prelude-injection blocks; behavior unchanged.
> - U.1.3 (one registry from inlined module; delete separate parse; expose to checker): LARGEST/RISKIEST in U.1 (~2-4d). Hard gate = detect-mode registry-diff (load_builtins vs from-inlined-module) must be empty before deleting; codegen emitted-C must stay byte-identical. The real hazard: std files used WITHOUT import (fence, gc namespaces) that the import path doesn't inline — these route through U.1.4 instead. Multi-day but bounded by byte-identical-C discipline, not open-ended.
> - U.1.4 (single declared-intrinsic table): MEDIUM-HIGH (~2-3d). Genuinely novel; risk = drift between the four `if name==X` codegen arms and the .nv signature files (gc.nv:47 admits manual sync). Reconciliation is finite (enumerate the arms). This is the bridge to U.2.5/U.6.
> - U.1.5 (route 3 checker sites): MEDIUM (~1-2d). is_known is the central gate; Fail/Detach/CancelToken provenance must be grep-proven first (riskiest names).
> - U.1.6 (removal): MEDIUM (~1d) but FULL regression required (soundness removal). Own commit.
> - U.1.7 (tests): SMALL-MEDIUM (~1d). Needs a minimal copied-std tree for the relocated-std fixture.
> - U.1.8 (docs): SMALL (~0.5d).
> 
> OVERALL: U.1 reworked is realistically completable as a production-grade phase, ~8-14 days. No single task is multi-week. The two real hazards (U.1.3 registry-diff, U.1.4 intrinsic drift) are de-risked into their own tasks with detect-mode/reconciliation gates. The phase is MORE valuable than the original framing because it actually removes the include_str! std list and the separate codegen std parse (the principle's core targets), rather than entrenching them. FLAG: U.1.4 (declared-intrinsic table) is the one piece that needs owner sign-off on the §2 exception for the intrinsic c-lowering BODIES (gc.collect→nova_gc_collect() has no .nv body and never can — it's a true compiler intrinsic), which is a legitimate, minimal, documented §2 exception per conventions:111-119.

### U.2+U.3 — Один реестр + резолв в чекере

> **Summary.** U.2 + U.3 of Plan 172.1 (unified type engine). Current state: Nova has FOUR independent type engines. The method/signature data is built in FOUR places: checker TypeCheckCtx.method_table/fn_decls (types/mod.rs:2505-2531, the build loop), rebuilt nearly-identically in BoundCtx (mod.rs:9282-9287) and CapabilityCtx (mod.rs:10867); plus codegen's real registry method_overloads: BTreeMap<(String,String),Vec<MethodSig>> (emit_c.rs:618, MethodSig def :12-39) populated in a preamble pre-pass (emit_c.rs:2389/3303/3498/3608/9560) and read at 90 sites. Builtin stdlib lives in a SEPARATE codegen-only ExternalRegistry (external_registry.rs:57) parsed from .nv — the checker does NOT read it (that is U.1, not yet done; plan-172-unified-type-engine branch == main, empty). U.2 merges the three checker tables + codegen method_overloads into ONE registry both layers read. U.3 moves overload/method resolution into the checker: the D84 free-fn resolver is inlined in emit_call (emit_c.rs:23150-23207), D124 cross-clock in emit_binop (emit_c.rs:20443-20474), and ~30 other inlined method-dispatch sites consult method_overloads directly; the named resolve_overload (emit_c.rs:11140) is DEAD CODE (zero callers). The checker already half-resolves via resolve_instance_method (mod.rs:10440) used by check_call_argbind (mod.rs:10120), but f1_check_call bails on instance methods with `_ => return` (mod.rs:6476). The checker→codegen channel ALREADY EXISTS: ModuleEnv (mod.rs:63-84) carries span-keyed side-tables (proven_index_sites: Vec<Span>) wired into the emitter via emitter.set_proven_*(&module_env.*) (main.rs:432-440) — U.3 reuses exactly this pattern for a span→resolved-callee table. Goal: one semantic pass resolves each call to a concrete callee; codegen consumes it; C never catches a type error.
>
> **Feasibility.** Realistically completable as a SEQUENCE of independently-committable refactors, but with two hard gates. GATE A — U.3 depends on a checker→codegen channel for the chosen callee. Good news: it already exists. ModuleEnv (mod.rs:63-84) is returned by check_module and already carries span-keyed side-tables (proven_index_sites) pushed into the emitter via set_proven_* (main.rs:432-440). U.3.1 reuses this exact, proven mechanism — this de-risks the single biggest architectural unknown and is why U.3 is feasible at all. GATE B — U.3.3 (instance-method resolution, esp. the hotspot Vec.push) needs the checker to SEE builtin signatures, which is U.1 (checker reads ExternalRegistry). U.1 is NOT done (plan-172-unified-type-engine branch == main, empty). Therefore U.3.3/U.3.5's BUILTIN coverage is soft-blocked on U.1; I scoped both to ship user-type-only first with a recorded [M-172-builtin-recv-pending-U1] gap, and explicitly noted the dependency rather than assuming U.1. SIZING: U.2.3 (checker swap, ~12 read-sites, 3 ctxs) and U.2.4 (codegen build swap, 90 read-sites kept read-only) are each multi-day but bounded — the discipline is byte-identical emitted-C + 0-regression-vs-clean-binary, which is verifiable, not open-ended. U.3.2/U.3.3 are the riskiest: they move whole error CLASSES from codegen-string/C-catch into checker diagnostics, which compiler-conventions §6 says MUST be measured in detect-mode before going fatal — each carries that instruction. The single most likely multi-day-by-itself task is U.3.3 (instance methods are pervasive in std); its blast-radius is genuinely unknown until detect-mode runs, so I'd treat the detect-mode count as a real go/no-go checkpoint, not a formality. The DEAD resolve_overload (zero callers) and the fact that real resolution is INLINED at ~30 sites is the central complication of U.3: there is no single function to move — codegen must instead be made to consult resolved_callees at each dispatch arm with fallback, which is why U.3 is decomposed per dispatch-family (free-fn, instance, operator) rather than as one cut. Const-fn (3rd engine) and sum-schema (4th) are intentionally OUT of U.2/U.3 scope (they are U.6).
>
> **Критерий приёмки фазы.** U.2 done when: (1) ONE signature/method registry (sig_registry.rs) is built by ONE pass and consumed by BOTH checker (TypeCheckCtx/BoundCtx/CapabilityCtx) and codegen (method_overloads) — the three duplicate checker build loops (mod.rs:2514,9286,10867) are deleted and their `method_table`/`fn_decls` fields removed; (2) the two hand-synced is_intrinsic_namespace lists (mod.rs:8706 ↔ emit_c.rs:23338) collapse to one; (3) dead resolve_overload (emit_c.rs:11140) removed and MethodSig single-defined; (4) emitted C is byte-identical to the clean binary across ≥8 plan dirs (mangling/order preserved) and full `nova test` shows 0 regressions vs clean binary. U.3 done when: (1) overload + instance/static + operator-method (D124) resolution happens in the checker, which records the chosen callee in ModuleEnv.resolved_callees (span-keyed, wired like proven_index_sites) and codegen CONSUMES it (no longer the first/only resolver — falls back only on recorded gaps); (2) `[E_NO_MATCHING_OVERLOAD]`, `[E_AMBIGUOUS_OVERLOAD]`, D124 cross-clock, and method-arg `[E_IMPLICIT_NARROWING]` are CLEAN CHECKER diagnostics (no codegen Err-strings, no CC-FAIL) — proven by negative fixtures in neg/ run with release nova `--compile-error`; (3) f1_check_call's instance `_ => return` (mod.rs:6476) is gone, replaced by real resolution (remaining `_` arms only cover principled-unresolvable cases, each under an [M-*] marker per §3). EVERY task: production-grade (no stubs/simplifications), conforms to compiler-conventions.md §0 (one source of truth), §1 (checks live in checker), §2 (no hardcoded Nova names — registry from .nv), §3 (no silent _ => return), §4 (spec-first: D311/D312 + error-index), §6 (blast-radius measured in detect-mode + verified against a stash+rebuild CLEAN binary, not a sibling), §7 (positive AND negative tests via release nova C-codegen pipeline); 0 regressions vs clean binary at every commit.

#### U.2.1 — Define unified signature-registry data type (single source of truth)
- **Что:** Introduce a new module `compiler-codegen/src/sig_registry.rs` defining a representation-neutral `SigRegistry` keyed by `(receiver: Option<String>, method_name)` → `Vec<SigEntry>`. `SigEntry` must carry EVERYTHING both layers need so neither re-derives: the raw `&FnDecl` (for the checker's TypeRef-level work: params with raw TypeRef, generics, receiver kind/mutability/consume, return TypeRef, variadic, defaults, spans) AND a lazily/eagerly computed codegen view (param C-types, return C-type, mangled c_name, is_instance/is_external/is_delegated/recv_mutable/variadic_last/param_defaults — the existing MethodSig fields). Do NOT delete MethodSig or the three checker tables yet; this task only ADDS the type + a builder skeleton with unit tests. Lifetime: mirror the existing `FnDeclArena` (mod.rs:2241) pattern so `&'a FnDecl` references stay valid. Document in a `[M-172-sig-registry]` marker that MethodSig will be folded into SigEntry.codegen_view in U.2.5.
- **Где:** NEW file compiler-codegen/src/sig_registry.rs; register module in compiler-codegen/src/lib.rs; reference shape from MethodSig (emit_c.rs:12-39), ExternalDecl (external_registry.rs:22-52), checker method_table type (mod.rs:2273).
- **Приёмка:** `cargo test -p nova-codegen sig_registry` passes new unit tests that: build a SigRegistry from a small parsed module with (a) a free fn, (b) two overloaded free fns, (c) an instance method, (d) a static method, (e) a `mut` receiver method — and assert key/arity/is_instance/recv_mutable/return are recorded correctly. Negative unit test: querying a missing (recv,method) returns empty. No behavior change to the compiler (registry not yet consumed). `cargo build` clean, full `nova test` sample 0 regressions vs clean binary.
- **Blast-radius:** Zero runtime behavior change (additive). Risk only if module wiring breaks build. Measure: `cargo build` + run plan11/plan172 sample fixtures before commit.
- **Deps:** none · **Risk:** Lifetime/arena design wrong → borrow errors. De-risk: copy the proven FnDeclArena invariant doc verbatim and unit-test reference stability after Vec growth.

#### U.2.2 — Single build-pass that produces the unified registry from a Module
- **Что:** Implement `SigRegistry::build(module: &Module, arena: &FnDeclArena) -> SigRegistry` that iterates `module.items` ONCE, registering every `Item::Fn` (free fn → key (None,name); receiver fn → key (Some(recv.type_name),name)), recording overloads, generics, receiver kind/mut/consume, variadic, defaults. This is the ONE loop replacing the three drifted checker loops (mod.rs:2514-2525, 9286-9307+, 10867+) — replicate every behavior those three currently have (e.g. TypeCheckCtx also records arity/types — keep arity/types build separate for now; only method/fn-decl tables are merged here). Mirror codegen's two-pass overload-count→mangle so c_name mangling matches emit_c.rs:3266-3303 exactly. Add a parity unit test comparing the unified table against a freshly-built TypeCheckCtx.method_table for a representative module (same keys, same overload counts, same FnDecl identity).
- **Где:** compiler-codegen/src/sig_registry.rs (build fn); parity-source = TypeCheckCtx::build (mod.rs:2505-2531), BoundCtx::build (mod.rs:9282+), CapabilityCtx::build (mod.rs:10867+), codegen mangling (emit_c.rs:3266-3303).
- **Приёмка:** Unit test asserts SigRegistry::build over a multi-item module yields identical (recv,method)→arity sets as the legacy three builds. Mangled c_names match codegen for overloaded + single-overload + variadic cases. `nova test` sample 0 regressions (registry still not consumed). Negative: a module with a receiver method and a free fn of the same name keep distinct keys (None vs Some(T)).
- **Blast-radius:** Still additive (not consumed). Risk: mangling divergence from codegen would surface in U.2.4. Measure by asserting c_name equality against MethodSig produced by the existing pre-pass on the same module.
- **Deps:** U.2.1 · **Risk:** Subtle per-table differences (e.g. CapabilityCtx walks all overloads, BoundCtx adds sum_variant_names) get lost. De-risk: enumerate each legacy build's side-effects in the task PR description and assert each in a unit test before any deletion.

#### U.2.3 — Checker consumes the unified registry; delete the three method_table/fn_decls builds
- **Что:** Build the SigRegistry ONCE in check_module_impl (mod.rs:105) and thread it (by reference) into TypeCheckCtx, BoundCtx, CapabilityCtx instead of each building its own `method_table`/`fn_decls`. Replace every read of `self.method_table`/`self.fn_decls` in those three ctxs with registry queries (preserve exact semantics: resolve_instance_method mod.rs:10440 inherent/extension priority, is_inherent_method, single-overload arity filter). Remove the three duplicate build loops and the now-unused `method_table`/`fn_decls` fields. Keep TypeCheckCtx.arity/types/type_method_map as-is (out of scope). This is a checker-internal refactor — ZERO new diagnostics, ZERO removed diagnostics.
- **Где:** mod.rs: check_module_impl :105; TypeCheckCtx fields :2271-2273 + build :2505; BoundCtx fields :9266-9267 + build :9282; CapabilityCtx fields :10815-10817 + build :10867; all `self.method_table`/`self.fn_decls` reads in those impls (resolve_instance_method :10440, check_call_argbind :10120, f1_check_call :6388/6395/6448, is_known_fn :2869, t_provides_method :7652).
- **Приёмка:** Full `nova test` (positive+negative sample ~1500) shows EXACTLY the same pass/fail set as the clean binary (0 regressions, 0 new passes) — proven by a clean baseline (NO `git stash` — temp-worktree/commit-reset) per compiler-conventions §7. `cargo build` clean; the three duplicate build loops gone; `method_table`/`fn_decls` fields removed from all three ctxs. Negative fixtures for arity/E7401/E7301 still fire identically.
- **Blast-radius:** Touches every checker site that reads method_table/fn_decls (~12 sites across 3 ctxs). Behavior must be byte-identical. Measure: diff full diagnostic output (stdout) of `nova test` against clean binary on the negative_capability + plan11 + plan46 + plan162 fixture sets.
- **Deps:** U.2.2 · **Risk:** resolve_instance_method's inherent-vs-extension priority subtly changes → false E7301/E7401 on std. De-risk: port that logic unchanged behind the registry query; add a regression-guard fixture per priority branch (inherent-wins, name-only-unique, ambiguous→skip).

> **ДЕКОМПОЗИЦИЯ U.2.3 (impl-разведка 2026-06-20).** Чтение живого чекера выявило два
> факта, которых нет в исходной формулировке U.2.3 — они меняют дизайн (но не цель).
> Соответствие [`compiler-conventions.md`](../compiler-conventions.md) §0/§1/§2.
>
> **Findings (сверено по коду worktree, не по номерам плана):**
> - **F1 — структурный mismatch представлений.** `SigRegistry.by_key` — ПЛОСКАЯ
>   `(Option<receiver>,name)→Vec<SigEntry>`. Чекер же читает ВЛОЖЕННУЮ
>   `method_table[type][method]` и делает то, что плоский ключ не умеет: возврат
>   ЗАИМСТВОВАННОЙ внутренней карты `method_table.get(type)` (нельзя «склеить на лету и
>   вернуть `&`»); полную итерацию `for (type,methods) in &method_table`
>   (`resolve_instance_method` mod.rs:10499); `contains_key(type)` (:3376/:3379); частый
>   паттерн «есть ли у типа метод с таким именем» — `method_table.get(t).map_or(false, |m|
>   m.keys().any(|k| k.trim_start_matches('@')==name))` (≥4×: :6731/:6784/:6899/:6934). →
>   Реестр ОБЯЗАН хранить вложенное base-представление (legacy-типы ДОСЛОВНО), а не
>   реконструировать из плоского ключа, иначе ломается borrow-модель и byte-identical.
> - **F2 — асимметрия синтеза (главный риск).** `TypeCheckCtx.method_table` = user-методы
>   **+ синтезированные auto-derive** (`register_synthesized_methods` mod.rs:2671, из
>   `synth_arena`); `BoundCtx`/`CapabilityCtx` — **только user**. Отдать «один реестр со
>   синтезом» всем трём → Bound/Cap начнут видеть `@equal`/`@hash`/… → потенциальный сдвиг
>   `check_satisfaction`/capability-резолва (§3-риск из de-risk-заметки U.2.3). Полезный
>   инвариант: синтез добавляет метод ТОЛЬКО если тип сам его не предоставляет (:2666) →
>   для пары `(type,method)` overloads приходят ЛИБО из base, ЛИБО из synth, не смешиваясь.
> - **F3 — перф (§2).** `CodegenView` (`type_ref_to_c` по всему merged-модулю) чекеру НЕ
>   нужен → расщепить build на дешёвый base-индекс (чекер) и отдельную CodegenView-populate
>   (codegen/U.2.4), чтобы не платить за C-маппинг на каждом `check_module`.
> - **F4 — тесты.** ~14 unit-тестов вызывают `TypeCheckCtx::build(&m,&arena)` и проверяют
>   `ctx.method_table` (mod.rs:22106–22352) — обновить на новый аксессор/локальный `sig`.
>
> **Решение по синтезу (open, фиксируется на U.2.3.3):**
> - **Вариант A (рекомендуемый, мин. риск):** общий реестр = **base-only** (Bound/Cap
>   получают ДОСЛОВНО то же, что строят сейчас → byte-identical тривиально). TypeCheckCtx
>   держит собственный `synth_methods`-overlay (синтез — его уникальная забота, не дубль
>   build-цикла). Маркер `[M-172.1-U2.3-synth-overlay]`. Дубль base-цикла устранён во всех
>   трёх; поле `method_table` уходит отовсюду, в TypeCheckCtx остаётся только `synth_methods`.
> - **Вариант B (чище по §0, дороже):** синтез внутрь общего реестра, отдать всем трём;
>   доказать корпусным byte-identical-C + diff-диагностик, что Bound/Cap НЕ затронуты; при
>   пустом diff — убрать поле и из TypeCheckCtx. Непустой diff → откат к A.
>
> **Под-шаги (каждый отдельный коммит, byte-identical-гейт):**
> - **U.2.3.1 (additive)** — расщепить `SigRegistry::build_from_module` → `build_base`
>   (дешёвый: плоский `by_key` БЕЗ CodegenView + вложенный base `method_table` + `fn_decls`,
>   один проход) + `populate_codegen_views` (для U.2.4). Добавить чекер-аксессоры
>   (`free_fns`/`method_overloads`/`methods_of`/`has_type`/iter), возвращающие legacy-типы
>   дословно. Реестр ещё НЕ потребляется. Unit-тесты на аксессоры. Гейт: `cargo test`, 0
>   изменений поведения.
> - **U.2.3.2 — Bound/Cap consume `&SigRegistry`.** `check_module_impl` строит `build_base`
>   ОДИН раз (до :696), передаёт в `BoundCtx::build`/`CapabilityCtx::build`; удалить их поля
>   `method_table`/`fn_decls` + build-циклы, читать через аксессоры. (base-only → дословно.)
>   Гейт: byte-identical C на ≥8 фикстурах + `nova test` сэмпл 0 регресс + diff диагностик
>   (особенно satisfaction/capability) = пусто.
> - **U.2.3.3 — TypeCheckCtx consume `&SigRegistry` + synth-overlay (вариант A/B решается
>   здесь).** Хелпер `type_has_method_named` (схлопывает :6731/:6784/:6899/:6934); `DeriveQuery`
>   читает base(`&sig`)+synth-so-far; удалить base-цикл, поле `method_table`→`synth_methods`.
>   Обновить unit-тесты (F4). Гейт: byte-identical **включая plan126 auto-derive** + diff
>   E73xx-диагностик = пусто.
> - **U.2.3.4 — docs/status/маркеры** ([M-172.1-U2.3-synth-overlay] при A), simplifications.md,
>   project-creation/discussion-log.
>
> **Byte-identical гейт (общий).** Baseline БЕЗ `git stash` (shared `.git` → опасно при
> параллельных агентах): реестр сейчас additive/не потребляется → HEAD ветки ДО U.2.3 = «чистый
> бинарь»; снять золотой C на нём. ≥8 фикстур обязаны покрывать зоны риска: auto-derive
> (plan126 — F2), inherent/extension (plan162 — приоритет `resolve_instance_method`), overloads
> (plan11), методы (plan46), str/Vec (lang-item+builtin-receiver), Option/Result (plan59), sync
> (plan103), + multi-file folder-module. Критерий: diff сгенерированного C = пусто; тот же
> pass/fail-набор; diff диагностик на neg (E7301/E7401/E7320/E7310/arity) = пусто.

#### U.2.4 — Codegen consumes the unified registry for method_overloads
- **Что:** Build/obtain the SigRegistry once in the codegen entry (CEmitter) and populate `method_overloads` FROM it (or replace `method_overloads` reads with registry queries returning the codegen view). Start by making the codegen pre-pass (emit_c.rs:2389/3303/3498/3608/9560) call into SigRegistry instead of re-deriving param C-types/mangling, so codegen and checker share ONE built table. Keep all 90 read-sites working by having the registry expose a `method_overloads`-shaped view (BTreeMap for determinism, per the :613 comment). Do NOT yet move resolution logic (that is U.3). ExternalRegistry builtin merge stays as today (it is U.1's job to feed it to the checker; here just ensure codegen's builtin entries still populate the shared registry the same way).
- **Где:** emit_c.rs: method_overloads field :618; pre-pass populators :2389,:3258-3303,:3430-3498,:3568-3608,:9560; CEmitter::new/emit_module entry (main.rs:413/447); determinism note emit_c.rs:613.
- **Приёмка:** Generated C is byte-identical to clean binary on a broad fixture sample (diff the emitted .c for plan11/plan46/plan91*/plan103* — must be identical; mangled names + emission order unchanged because BTreeMap determinism preserved). Full `nova test` 0 regressions vs clean binary. Negative: overloaded free-fn `no matching overload` still emitted by the unchanged inlined resolver.
- **Blast-radius:** emit_c.rs is hot and method_overloads read at 90 sites — but this task only changes WHO BUILDS the map, not who reads it, so reads are untouched. Measure: `diff` emitted C output dir vs clean binary across ≥8 plan dirs; any divergence = mangling/order drift to fix.
- **Deps:** U.2.2 · **Risk:** Emission order changes → latent prelude init-order bugs resurface (the :613 warning). De-risk: keep BTreeMap key+iteration identical; assert C-output byte-equality before commit, not just test pass/fail.

> **РАЗВЕДКА U.2.4 (2026-06-20) — исходная формулировка byte-identical-НЕВЫПОЛНИМА, требует переформулировки.**
> Чтение фактического построения `method_overloads` (emit_c.rs) выявило два факта, делающих
> «standalone SigRegistry → populate `method_overloads` из неё» byte-identical невозможным.
> Соответствие [`compiler-conventions.md`](../compiler-conventions.md) §0/§4 (spec-first, не ломать byte-identical).
>
> **F5 — `method_overloads` строится из 5+ ИСТОЧНИКОВ с РАЗНЫМИ mangling-схемами:**
> - (a) **ExternalRegistry builtins** (emit_c.rs:2374) — `MethodSig` из `ExternalDecl` (c_name уже посчитан в ER через `mangle_method_c_name`); `is_external=true`, `variadic_last=false`, defaults=None.
> - (b) **free-fn D84** (emit_c.rs:3189–3309) — sentinel-key `("",name)`; base = `free_fn_c_name(name)` (учитывает `c_literal_extern_fns` / `file_priv_fn_c_names` / `fn_module_map`→`mangle_free_fn` для модульных), суффикс overload = по **всем** `param_c_types` (sanitized C, joined); `existing_count` (incremental).
> - (c) **receiver methods** (emit_c.rs:3311–3498) — key `(receiver_type_c_ident, name)`; base = `Nova_{c_ident}_{consume|method|static}_{name}`; суффикс overload = **все** `param_c_types` (sanitized); `__mut`/`__ro` tiebreak (Plan 135); **erasure** `erased_type_ref_c` для generic-recv; `type_ref_to_c` через `self`-context (`current_receiver_type`).
> - (d) **embed-proxy D39** (emit_c.rs:3568–3608) — синтезированные `is_delegated=true` proxy (НЕ из module.items).
> - (e) **mono / прочее** (emit_c.rs:5650, 9560) — моно-инстансы генериков (`Vec____int`), генерятся при codegen, НЕ в module.items.
>
> **F6 — SigRegistry mangling (U.2.1/2.2) — УПРОЩЁННАЯ, совпадает с codegen ТОЛЬКО для single-overload concrete-recv:**
> `mangle_method_c_name` + `last_param_suffix` дают `Nova_{raw_type}_{name}` (+ `_{last-param-Nova-type}` при total≥2).
> Расходится с codegen-схемой по ОСЯМ: суффикс overload (last-param-**Nova** ↔ all-param-**C** sanitized);
> нет `__mut`/`__ro` tiebreak; нет erasure (generic-recv); `raw type_name` ↔ `receiver_type_c_ident`;
> free-fn base всегда `nova_fn_` ↔ `free_fn_c_name` (modular/file-priv/literal). Parity-тест U.2.2 был
> именно для совпадающего кейса (extern `AtomicI64.new` — single, concrete). Плюс `ExternalRegistry::type_ref_to_c`
> (standalone) ≠ `CEmitter::type_ref_to_c` (state-aware: `generic_types`/mono/receiver-context) — §0 «type→C трижды».
>
> **Корень.** codegen mangling/type-mapping ЗАВИСЯТ от состояния `CEmitter` (generic_types, mono-worklist,
> current_receiver_type, fn_module_map, file-priv). Standalone `SigRegistry::build_from_module(module)` этого
> состояния НЕ имеет → её CodegenView не может воспроизвести codegen c_name byte-identical для
> overloaded/generic/mut/modular методов. Наивная замена источника → масса c_name-drift → CC-FAIL/мис-диспатч.
>
> **Переформулировка (развилка для владельца — 3 пути):**
> - **(1) build-inside-CEmitter:** строить `SigRegistry` ВНУТРИ `CEmitter` (доступ к `self.type_ref_to_c` +
>   единый mangler, учитывающий все оси: all-param-C suffix, mut-tiebreak, erasure-флаг, free_fn_c_name).
>   SigRegistry становится индексом ПОВЕРХ codegen-derivation (не независимый билд). Byte-identical достижим;
>   `method_overloads`-populators (a)…(e) сводятся к ОДНОМУ код-пути наполнения общего реестра.
> - **(2) unify-mangler-only:** не менять источник; вынести ОДИН mangler, который зовут И codegen-populators,
>   И `SigRegistry` (CodegenView mangling переписать под полную codegen-схему). Локальная §0-унификация mangling
>   без смены владельца построения. Меньше риск, частичный §0.
> - **(3) defer:** U.2.4 (полное «codegen потребляет реестр») зависит по существу от U.4/U.5 (typed IR, где типы
>   уже резолвлены чекером и erasure/state на codegen-слое не нужны) + U.6 (collapse `type_ref_to_c`×3). Отложить
>   U.2.4 за них; сейчас закрыть достижимое: U.2.5 (fold MethodSig в CodegenView как ЕДИНЫЙ тип + удалить мёртвый
>   `resolve_overload`) — это не требует смены источника и даёт реальный §0-выигрыш.
>
> Рекомендация: **(1)** как целевая (настоящий §0), но крупная; **(3)** для немедленного прогресса (U.2.5 landable
> сейчас, U.2.4-impl за U.4/U.5/U.6). `[M-172.1-U2.4-mangling-fragmented]`.

#### U.2.5 — Unify intrinsic-namespace list + fold MethodSig into the registry; remove dead resolve_overload
- **Что:** (a) Replace the two hand-synced `is_intrinsic_namespace` lists (checker mod.rs:8706 ↔ codegen guard emit_c.rs:23338) with ONE shared function/const in sig_registry.rs (or a shared util), consumed by both — removing the 'must match' manual-sync comment. (b) Delete the dead `resolve_overload` (emit_c.rs:11140, zero callers). (c) Fold `MethodSig` into `SigEntry.codegen_view` (or make MethodSig a type alias produced by the registry) so there is one definition. This finalizes 'one registry, both layers consume, no manual sync' (U.2 acceptance).
- **Где:** mod.rs:8706 (is_intrinsic_namespace); emit_c.rs:23338-23344 (codegen guard list); emit_c.rs:11140 (dead resolve_overload); MethodSig def emit_c.rs:12-39 + its construction sites.
- **Приёмка:** grep shows ONE intrinsic-namespace list (the two old sites reference the shared one). `resolve_overload` gone, `cargo build` clean (confirms zero callers). MethodSig single-defined. Full `nova test` 0 regressions vs clean binary. Negative: a call on an intrinsic namespace (`gc.collect()`, `Time.now()`) still routes through the same codegen dispatch (fixture unchanged).
- **Blast-radius:** Small, surgical. Risk: the two intrinsic lists were already drifted (e.g. one has `Duration`, check both) — unifying may add/remove one name from one side's behavior. Measure: diff the two literal lists first; if they differ, that difference is a latent bug to resolve explicitly (document in marker).
- **Deps:** U.2.3, U.2.4 · **Risk:** Lists differ today → unification silently changes routing. De-risk: enumerate both lists, reconcile each name with a test, document the reconciliation in `[M-172-intrinsic-namespace-unify]`.

#### U.3.1 — Add the resolved-callee channel: ModuleEnv side-table + emitter setter (no resolution yet)
- **Что:** Add `pub resolved_callees: HashMap<Span, ResolvedCallee>` to `ModuleEnv` (mod.rs:63-84) where `ResolvedCallee` records the chosen callee for a Call site: c_name (mangled), is_instance, receiver type, param C-types, return C-type (enough for codegen to lower without re-resolving). Add `emitter.set_resolved_callees(&module_env.resolved_callees)` wiring in main.rs alongside the existing `set_proven_*` calls. Leave the map EMPTY for now and have codegen treat 'absent span' = fall back to today's inlined resolution. This establishes the channel exactly like proven_index_sites (mod.rs:73, main.rs:434) with zero behavior change.
- **Где:** ModuleEnv mod.rs:63-84; main.rs:347 (module_env), :432-440 (set_proven_* block — add set_resolved_callees here); new setter near emit_c.rs:1767-1805 set_proven_* family; new emitter field near :580.
- **Приёмка:** `cargo build` clean; map is empty so `nova test` is byte-identical to clean binary (0 regressions). Unit test: ModuleEnv default has empty resolved_callees; setter stores and emitter exposes it. The wiring mirrors proven_index_sites (verified by reading main.rs:434).
- **Blast-radius:** Additive, zero behavior change (empty table). Measure: full sample `nova test` parity + emitted-C byte-diff (must be identical).
- **Deps:** U.2.4 · **Risk:** Span as map key may collide if spans aren't unique per call site. De-risk: assert in a unit test that distinct Call exprs in a sample module have distinct spans; if not, key on (Span, callee-form) — decide before populating in U.3.2.

#### U.3.2 — Checker resolves free-fn overloads (D84) and populates resolved_callees + emits no-matching-overload/ambiguous
- **Что:** In the checker, for `ExprKind::Call` with an Ident/Path callee that the SigRegistry shows as OVERLOADED, resolve by argument types using the registry (port the D84 filter from emit_c.rs:23153-23207: arity + param-type match, dup-c_name collapse, genuine ambiguity = error). Record the chosen callee into ModuleEnv.resolved_callees by the call span. Emit the diagnostics IN THE CHECKER: `[E_NO_MATCHING_OVERLOAD]` (new code) on 0 candidates, `[E_AMBIGUOUS_OVERLOAD]` on >1 distinct. To compare arg types the checker needs C-typed args — reuse the registry codegen-view param types and the checker's existing type inference; where the checker cannot infer an arg type (best-effort gap), DO NOT resolve/record (leave to codegen fallback) and mark with `[M-172-checker-argtype-gap]` rather than guessing. Then make codegen's free-fn resolver (emit_c.rs:23150) FIRST consult resolved_callees and only fall back to its inlined logic on absent span.
- **Где:** Checker: f1_check_call (mod.rs:6367) or a new resolve pass in check_module_impl; new diag codes in spec 09-tooling.md. Codegen consume: emit_c.rs:23150-23207 (free-fn arm of emit_call). D84 source logic: emit_c.rs:23153-23207.
- **Приёмка:** `g(int)/g(str)` called with `g(bool)` → checker emits `[E_NO_MATCHING_OVERLOAD]` (clean Nova diagnostic, span on the call), NOT a codegen `no matching overload`/CODEGEN-FAIL. Genuine ambiguity → `[E_AMBIGUOUS_OVERLOAD]`. Positive: monomorphic overload set resolves and codegen emits the SAME c_name as before (emitted-C byte-identical where the checker resolved). Negative fixtures in `neg/` via `--compile-error`. Full `nova test` 0 regressions vs clean binary; spec D-block + error-index updated.
- **Blast-radius:** Moves a class of errors from codegen-string to checker-diagnostic; any overloaded free-fn call across std/tests now resolves in checker. Measure (detect-mode first per §6): count call sites where checker-resolution disagrees with codegen-resolution BEFORE flipping to fatal; reconcile each. The 24 overload-touching nova_tests dirs are the primary corpus.
- **Deps:** U.3.1 · **Risk:** Checker arg-type inference weaker than codegen's infer_expr_c_type → false E_NO_MATCHING_OVERLOAD. De-risk: only resolve when ALL arg types are known to the checker; otherwise defer to codegen (recorded gap). Run detect-mode blast-radius before making it fatal.

#### U.3.3 — Checker resolves instance/static method calls; remove f1_check_call `_ => return`
- **Что:** Extend the U.3.2 resolution to `ExprKind::Member`/`Path` method calls using SigRegistry + resolve_instance_method (mod.rs:10440) for receiver-type inference, INCLUDING builtin methods (depends on U.1 so the registry contains Vec.push/str.* — if U.1 is not merged, gate the builtin-receiver branch behind a recorded `[M-172-builtin-recv-pending-U1]` and resolve only user-type receivers). Record chosen callee into resolved_callees. Replace `f1_check_call`'s instance-method `_ => return` (mod.rs:6476) with real resolution + arg type-checking (this is the soundness hole from compiler-conventions §3). Make the ~main codegen instance-dispatch sites (emit_c.rs:26931-26983 instance arm, :25249 primitive-ext arm, :23276 self-call arm) consult resolved_callees first, falling back to inlined logic on absent span.
- **Где:** mod.rs: f1_check_call instance arm :6473-6476 (the `_ => return`); resolve_instance_method :10440. Codegen consume: emit_c.rs:26920-26983 (instance method dispatch), :25247-25300 (primitive ext), :23230-23316 (self-call). Builtin source: ExternalRegistry (U.1).
- **Приёмка:** `obj.method(arg)` with a type-mismatched arg → checker `[E7301]`/`[E_IMPLICIT_NARROWING]` (the Plan 172.2 hotspot `vec_u32.push(int)` once U.1 lands) instead of CC-FAIL/silent. `f1_check_call` no longer has a bare `_ => return` for instance methods (the `_` arm only covers genuinely-unresolvable receivers, marked). Positive: existing method calls resolve to identical c_names (emitted-C byte-identical on resolved sites). Full `nova test` 0 regressions vs clean binary; negative fixtures in `neg/`.
- **Blast-radius:** Largest of U.3 — instance methods are everywhere in std. Measure in detect-mode: count instance-call sites where checker-resolution diverges from codegen; reconcile before fatal. Without U.1, builtin-receiver methods (push) are excluded → smaller initial radius (user-type methods only).
- **Deps:** U.3.2; SOFT-deps U.1 (builtin receivers) — if U.1 absent, ship user-type-only with a recorded gap. · **Risk:** resolve_instance_method is best-effort; removing `_ => return` could surface false errors on generic/alias/unknown receivers. De-risk: permissive skip (no resolution, no error) on generic-param/alias/unknown receivers per §3, each commented; detect-mode blast-radius run mandatory before fatal.

#### U.3.4 — Move D124 cross-clock and binop method-dispatch resolution to the checker
- **Что:** Port the D124 cross-clock rejection (emit_c.rs:20443-20474: `-` with no matching `@minus` overload on receiver) and the operator-method dispatch (`==`→@equal, `<`→@compare, `|`/`&`→@or/@and) resolution decisions into the checker, recording the chosen operator-method callee into resolved_callees keyed by the binop span. Emit the D124 rejection as a clean checker diagnostic (`[E_CROSS_CLOCK_ARITH]` or reuse existing) instead of the codegen `Err(...)` string. Codegen's emit_binop consults resolved_callees for the operator-method c_name first, falling back to inlined dispatch on absent span. Keep the generic-mono `____`-split path in codegen (it is mono-substitution, lowering — stays).
- **Где:** emit_c.rs: D124 `-`/@minus :20443-20474; @equal :20526-20542; @compare ordering :20543-20556+; @or/@and :20499-20521. Checker: extend the U.3.2/U.3.3 resolve pass to BinOp exprs.
- **Приёмка:** `Timestamp - Monotonic` (no cross-clock @minus) → clean checker diagnostic, NOT a codegen Err string. `a == b` on a type with user `@equal` resolves to the same c_name (emitted-C identical). Full `nova test` 0 regressions vs clean binary; D-block + error-index updated for any new/renamed code; negative fixture in `neg/`.
- **Blast-radius:** Narrow (operator methods on record/sum types — Duration/Timestamp/Monotonic + user @equal/@compare). Measure: diff emitted C for plan65/plan103* (clock/sync) + any @equal fixtures; assert identical c_names; assert D124 negative fixture now reports a Nova error code not a codegen string.
