- **Deps:** U.3.3 · **Risk:** Operator dispatch has many fall-through paths (generic mono, synthesis-from-@compare) — moving the wrong one breaks lowering. De-risk: move ONLY the resolution DECISION + diagnostic; leave all mono-substitution/synthesis in codegen; byte-diff emitted C.

#### U.3.5 — Method-arg narrowing in the checker (Plan 172.2 closeout) + U.3 acceptance gate
- **Что:** With method calls now resolved in the checker (U.3.3), wire the existing `is_int_narrowing`/`Compat::Narrowing`/`[E_IMPLICIT_NARROWING]` machinery (already used for free-fn args in f1_check_call mod.rs:6528) onto resolved method-call args — closing the canonical hole `vec_u32.push(int_var)`. Permissive on alias/newtype/generic/unknown per §3. This is the concrete Plan 172.2 deliverable that U.1+U.2+U.3 unlock. Run the full blast-radius (Plan 172.2 Ф.2 expects ~375 push(int) sites in std) in detect-mode, then this task ONLY enables it + adds tests; the std migration (`as u32`) is tracked as Plan 172.2 Ф.3 (separate, not in this phase's scope) OR done here if radius is small.
- **Где:** mod.rs: f1_check_call narrowing arm reused :6528-6544; method resolution from U.3.3; is_int_narrowing/assignable :7748; Compat enum.
- **Приёмка:** `vec_u32.push(int_var)` → `[E_IMPLICIT_NARROWING]`; `vec_u32.push(int_var as u32)` → OK; widening `Vec[int].push(u8_var)` → OK; builtin coverage requires U.1. Positive+negative fixtures via release nova `--compile-error` in `neg/`. After migration/flagging, std+nova_tests green, 0 false positives vs clean binary. Spec D311 + error-index updated.
- **Blast-radius:** Potentially ~375 std sites (codecs/crypto/unicode push(int)). Measure FIRST in detect-mode (non-fatal count) per §6; if large, gate enablement behind completed migration (Plan 172.2 Ф.3) rather than red std.
- **Deps:** U.3.3 (method resolution); SOFT-dep U.1 (builtin Vec.push receiver) · **Risk:** Enabling before migrating std turns std red. De-risk: detect-mode count is the gate; do not flip fatal until migration done or radius==0; permissive on generic/alias prevents false positives.

### U.4+U.5 — Единый inference + единое представление

> **Summary.** U.4 (unified expression inference) and U.5 (unified width/modifier representation) of Plan 172.1. CURRENT STATE: Nova has TWO independent expression-inference engines over different representations. Checker: `infer_expr_type` (types/mod.rs:7894-8058, ~165 lines, returns Option<TypeRef>) — best-effort, covers literals/idents/As/a-few-Call-shapes, returns None for most calls/members/index/binary. Codegen: `infer_expr_c_type` (emit_c.rs:35718-38805, ~3090 lines, returns C-string) — the REAL engine: its Call arm (36250-38287, ~2000 lines) contains the actual method/overload resolver (method_overloads:618, infer_mono_method_ret_with_args, resolve_overload:11140) and is coupled to codegen-only name-keyed side-tables (var_types:521, array_element_types, generic_type_instance_info, closure_param_type_overrides, pattern_binding_overrides, mono C-name string decoding). 275 call sites in emit_c.rs + uses in external_registry.rs/desugar.rs. CRITICAL BLOCKER for U.4: `Expr` is `struct { kind, span }` (ast/mod.rs:1993) with NO type-annotation field — there is no typed IR today; "C-strings derive FROM the annotated IR type" requires building that annotation infrastructure first, and the resolver must already live in the checker (U.3). U.5: `Ty` (enum :19, int-collapse via ty_of_ref:13145) and `TyCat` (enum :8653, cat_of_depth:8349 int-arm collapses all int widths to TyCat::Int, drops generics) both lose width/sign; three width helpers (sized_int_bounds:8540, int_width_rank:8586, is_int_narrowing:8619) plus raw-TypeRef bolt-ons (is_int_narrowing at assignable:7877-7885; generic_arg_mismatch raw pass at f1_check_call:6562) were added to recover the lost width. TyCat=46 uses, Ty::=28, cat_of*=22 uses in types/mod.rs.
>
> **Feasibility.** NOT realistically completable as a single production-grade phase without splitting — and two tasks are multi-week by themselves. HARD ORDERING REALITY: U.4 is NOT independent of U.1-U.3. The premise of U.4 ('C-strings derive FROM the annotated IR type') has two missing prerequisites in the current code: (a) there is NO typed IR — `Expr` is `{ kind, span }` (ast/mod.rs:1993), no type-annotation field exists, so U.4.1 must FIRST build the annotation substrate (a non-trivial keystone, gated on proving span-uniqueness vs needing a threaded ExprId because desugar.rs clones spans); and (b) the REAL inference engine `infer_expr_c_type` (emit_c.rs:35718, ~3090 lines) does its work IN a ~2000-line Call arm (36250-38287) that IS the method/overload resolver — so U.4.3 cannot be attempted until U.3 has moved resolve_overload/method dispatch into the checker. FLAGGED MULTI-WEEK: U.4.3 ('move resolution result into IR / collapse the Call arm') is multi-week on its own — 275 call sites, ~2000 lines, entangled with mono-instantiation SIDE-EFFECTS (lazy typedef emission, register_mono_tuple) that must NOT be skipped when reading an annotation, and it is HARD-gated on U.3. U.5.4 ('replace Ty/TyCat everywhere, delete helpers') is also multi-week — 96 usage sites and `Ty` is `pub` (possible nova-lsp/cross-crate consumers → may need a facade, not deletion). RECOMMENDATION: schedule U.5 BEFORE U.4 (U.5.1's structured type is the natural annotation carrier for U.4.1, and U.5 is self-contained within the checker with no U.3 dependency), and do NOT start U.4.3/U.4.4 until U.2+U.3 are merged and stable. U.4.1/U.4.2 and all of U.5 can proceed independently now. Each listed task is individually committable+testable; the two multi-week tasks (U.4.3, U.5.4) are flagged and should themselves be re-decomposed (the a/b/c/d sub-staging and arm-by-arm batches are noted in their entries) when picked up.
>
> **Критерий приёмки фазы.** U.4 done when: (1) exactly ONE expression-inference implementation exists — the semantic pass annotates every Expr with a resolved type, and codegen's `infer_expr_c_type` is a thin lowering (`resolved_type_to_c(ir.type_of(expr))`) with NO independent resolution/inference logic (grep-provable; the ~2000-line Call-arm resolver is gone from the type path); (2) C-type strings derive FROM the IR annotation, proven by a full-corpus equivalence assert showing 0 mismatches and an empty emitted-.c diff vs the clean binary; (3) type errors that previously surfaced as CODEGEN-FAIL/CC-FAIL now surface as clean checker diagnostics. U.5 done when: (1) ONE structured type carries width/sign/L1-L3, replacing Ty/TyCat int-collapse and the three standalone width helpers (TyCat/cat_of*/int_width_rank/sized_int_bounds consolidated — grep-provable); (2) the raw-TypeRef 'recover lost width' bolt-ons at assignable:7877 and f1_check_call:6562 are removed (folded into the unified compare); (3) width/sign/modifiers are uniformly available. BOTH phases: production-grade with no simplifications; conforms to compiler-conventions.md §0 (single source of truth), §1 (checks live in checker), §2 (no hardcoded stdlib — only the sanctioned primitive width/sign exception, marked), §3 (no silent _=>return); every rule has positive AND negative tests via RELEASE nova (C-codegen pipeline, EXPECT_COMPILE_ERROR for negatives, neg/ folder-modules); 0 regressions vs a clean binary built from stash (per §6 verification); spec D312 + 09-tooling error-index + simplifications.md updated.

> **CROSS-PLAN: Plan 181 (D325 Result-everywhere) Ф.2b-блокеры = конкретные acceptance-кейсы U.4 (зафиксировано 2026-06-25).**
> Plan 181 (единый fallible-контракт std, `Result`-everywhere) при `.nv`-миграции (base64/json/complex) наткнулся
> на codegen-баги, чья «компиляторная» часть (Ф.2b) ОТЛОЖЕНА. Каждый = ровно анти-паттерн «codegen **угадывает**
> return-C-тип метода вместо чтения из канала», который удаляет U.4 (conventions §0/§1/§10). Plan 181 §6 ждёт
> их фикса «отдельным compiler-агентом» — но по §0 (один источник истины) это **работа U.4**, НЕ параллельный
> фикс тех же `emit_c.rs`-хардкодов (иначе два агента чинят одни return-type-хардкоды = фрагментация, против
> которой и U.4). **Заклеймить за U.4 как реальные (из живой std-миграции) regression/acceptance-фикстуры:**
> - **`[M-181-result-over-named-tuple-codegen]`** — `Result`/`Vec` над named-tuple (`type Complex(re,im)`) →
>   wrapper-struct использует `NovaTuple_Complex` ДО его typedef (forward-ref) → `unknown type name`; родств.
>   D123/D216. → **U.4.3** — это ТОТ ЖЕ tuple-mono-registration hazard, что **Gap B-tuple** (net
>   `split→(R,W)`/`recv_from→Result[(str,Addr)]`, U.1.3b §9-строка). ОДИН фикс (типизированный IR для
>   tuple/Result-регистрации) закрывает оба.
> - **`[M-181-ifexpr-value-materialize-codegen]`** ✅ **RESOLVED 2026-06-26 (`836befcb`)** — `else if`-цепочка
>   с fluent `-> @`-хвостами (`out.push(..)`) и диверджащей финальной веткой → каст `(NovaArray*)(nova_unit)`
>   CC-FAIL (base64 `decode_with`). **Корень УТОЧНЁН (НЕ «receiver-vs-return» — `push` fluent, легитимно `Vec*`):**
>   рассинхрон emit/infer. `infer_If` (`emit_c.rs:38399`) НЕ имел fallback'а unit-доминирования
>   `[M-codegen-fluent-tail-if-unify]`, который есть в `emit_if_expr`, хотя арм требует «must match emit_if_expr's
>   choice» (R3) → вложенный if эмитит unit, infer даёт `Vec*` → внешний result-temp `Vec*` ← unit = CC-FAIL.
>   Фикс: `infer_If` зеркалит `emit_if_expr` (§0 один резолвер, R3). **Это R3-repair legacy-пути, НЕ U.4-канальный
>   флип** (первичная привязка к U.4.4/U.4.5 опиралась на неточный диагноз маркера 181). Гейт: §7.5 0 регресс,
>   §0 GOLD multiset-.c 5 диров IDENTICAL, фикстура `cgfix_fluent_tail_if/chain`.
> - **`[M-181-anon-record-in-ctor-arg-codegen]`** ✅ **RESOLVED 2026-06-26 (`c724de7a`)** — анон record-литерал
>   в позиции аргумента обёртки (`Ok({ tok, line, col })`) терял target-тип (прямой `return {..}` коэрсил по D55).
>   **Оказался ЛОКАЛЬНЫМ codegen target-propagation фиксом, НЕ полным RecordLit-резолвером** (как и допускала эта
>   врезка): contextual Ok/Err-арм `emit_call` уже несёт разрешённый payload-C-тип из канала (`novares_ok_err(&rt)`)
>   → ставим `expected_record_type` вокруг emit аргумента (зеркало D55-механизма). Byte-identical для не-анон-record
>   аргументов; разблокировал json ПАСТ анон-record (упирается в downstream erasure [M-91.13]). Полный
>   RecordLit-резолвер (sum/generic/value-контекст, 66% дивергенция) остаётся **U.4.5**. См. §9-строку.
> - **`emit_c.rs:38081-38082`/`:34040-34041` (`parse_int`→хардкод `NovaOpt_nova_int`), `:37724-37753`
>   (`read_X`→unboxed), `:27160`/`:27224` (builtins `int/f64.try_parse`)** — return-C-тип-хардкоды, блокирующие
>   D325-rename `parse.nv`/`read_buffer.nv`/builtins. → **U.4.5** (codegen читает method-return из канала →
>   хардкоды удаляются). Plan 171 (`int.parse(s, radix)→Result`, фикс truncation-бага `i8.try_from("999")→-25`)
>   выровнен под D325, его Ф.2b ждёт того же U.4.5.
>
> **Двунаправленная связь:** U.4.3 + U.4.5 разблокируют Plan 181 Ф.2b (и Plan 171 Ф.2b); 181-баги = готовые
> acceptance-кейсы U.4 из реальной миграции (звучнее синтетических). D325 на сам тип-движок не влияет
> (конвенция нейминга std); net/sync-срезы U.1.3b им НЕ затронуты (net уже Result-everywhere; sync под D325
> не мигрируется). При работе над U.4.3/U.4.5 — cross-ref эти маркеры в §9-строках как фикстуры.

> **КАРТА U.4 (§7 шаг 1, 4 Explore-агента по worktree, 2026-06-20).** Точки интеграции сверены по
> коду ветки (номера пост-U.5; plan-номера устарели). Соответствие §0/§1/§3.
>
> **M1 — две inference-машины.** Чекер: `infer_expr_type` (types/mod.rs:8442–8607, ~166 стр,
> `-> Option<TypeRef>`, ~18 арм handled, остальное `None`; 16 read-only callers — readonly/priv/
> narrowing/pattern, НЕ codegen). Codegen: `infer_expr_c_type` (emit_c.rs:35597–38692, ~3119 стр,
> `-> String`) — НАСТОЯЩИЙ движок, 42 арма; **Call-арм :36129–37044 = 916 стр** содержит весь
> резолв перегрузок/методов/mono. Leaf+operator (литералы/Binary/Unary/As/Is) ~100 стр; структурные
> (Member :38382 / Index :35963 / Match :38272 / RecordLit/ArrayLit/Block/Ident) ~1155 стр.
>
> **M2 — carrier ⚠ НЕПОЛОН (superseded by [D315](../../spec/decisions/02-types.md#d315-resolvedtype--единый-канонический-носитель-типа-plan-1721-2026-06-21), 2026-06-21).**
> `ResolvedType` (types/mod.rs:37–63) несёт width/sign (`Scalar`), `Float`, `Named{name,args}`
> (generic-args сохранены), `TypedPtr`, `Array`/`Tuple`/`Func`; умеет восстановить C-имя (`int_name()`).
> ~~Достаточен как носитель типа выражения для U.4.1.~~ **ПЕРЕСМОТРЕНО:** достаточен ТОЛЬКО для
> примитивов; для non-primitive C-типов **лосси** (спайк 2026-06-21): `from_type_ref` берёт
> `path.last()` (теряет модуль), схлопывает `*mut`-форму `Pointer(Mut)` в `TypedPtr(Ro,…)`,
> разворачивает L2 `readonly`. Цель D315 — обогатить до lossless-canonical (U.5.5) и опускать одним
> `resolved_type_to_c`. См. врезку «РЕОРГ U.4 (2026-06-21, D315)» ниже.
>
> **M3 — канал чекер→codegen есть, но НЕ для типов/callee.** `ModuleEnv` (types/mod.rs:461–483,
> `#[derive(Debug,Default)]`) несёт только `proven_*` Span-таблицы; провод — main.rs:430–441
> (`emitter.set_proven_*(&module_env.*)`, конвертит `span.start→usize` в HashSet). `resolved_callees`/
> `resolved_types` НЕ добавлены: U.3.1/U.3.3 пока лишь ЭМИТЯТ диагностику, выбранный overload codegen'у
> НЕ передают. Это тот самый канал, что переиспользует U.4.1.
>
> **M4 — 🔑 KEYSTONE: span-ключ ДОКАЗАННО небезопасен → нужен `ExprId`.** `Expr={kind,span}`
> (ast/mod.rs), поля id нет, `ExprId` в крейте нет. `Span` (diag.rs:26–33, `{start,end,file_id}`,
> Copy/Hash/Eq) — хороший ключ, НО spans НЕ уникальны на живых Expr (коллизии доказаны кодом):
> (a) parser `wrap_loop_with_preentry_check` (parser/mod.rs:9148–9162) — `For` и обёртка-`Block`
> делят span; (b) desugar `build_map_block` (desugar.rs:296–607) — `[k:v]` синтезирует ~15–20 Expr
> (Ident/TurboFish/Member/Call×N/For/Block), ВСЕ со span исходного MapLit; (c) `build_record_map_block`
> (desugar.rs:193–281) — то же. Разные Expr → разные типы → span-таблица коллизирует. **Вердикт:
> U.4.1 вводит `ExprId` (assign в `Expr::new`).** Доп.условие mono: тела генериков КЛОНИРУЮТСЯ под
> инстансы → `ExprId` при клоне **СОХРАНЯЕТСЯ** (тот же id ⇒ та же generic-аннотация); аннотация —
> **generic-уровня**, конкретику mono подставляет codegen (легитимный лоуэринг). СПАЙК перед коммитом
> дизайна: подтвердить ExprId через parser→desugar→mono (clone сохраняет id) на 2–3 фикстурах.
>
> **M5 — Call-арм = inference + оркестратор mono (U.4.3 обязан расщепить).** При выводе типа арм
> МУТИРУЕТ состояние: `register_mono_tuple` (:35699), `generic_type_instance_info`-insert +
> `generic_type_worklist.push` (:36192–36200), `register_generic_instances_in_typeref` (:36788,
> :37272), install/restore циклы `pattern_binding_overrides`/`type_subst_overrides`. U.4.3 разделяет
> SIDE-EFFECT-регистрацию (остаётся в codegen) и TYPE-derivation (уходит в чтение IR); наивное «читаем
> аннотацию» пропустит typedef'ы → CC-FAIL.
>
> **M6 — fallback census.** Exhaustive grep: **~126 сайтов** дефолт-C-типа (`nova_int`×96,
> `nova_unit`×27): ~40 в `infer_expr_c_type`, ~50 в `emit_expr`, ~30 в утилитах; ~45–50 masking-a-gap
> (напр. `.strip_prefix().unwrap_or("nova_int")` на элементах Vec/Option/Array → мис-диспатч). §1
> называет «~78» — РАСХОЖДЕНИЕ с конвенцией (census считал и `nova_unit`/широкие паттерны); вынесено
> владельцу, нужен узкий пересчёт по определению §1 (`nova_int` в inference-путях) ПЕРЕД трактовкой 126
> как авторитет. Конвенцию НЕ правлю молча (governance).
>
> **M6.1 — 169.2 fix-каталог = ТЕСТ-КОРПУС для U.4 (анализ 2026-06-21, по запросу владельца).**
> `docs/plan-169.2-compiler-fixes.md` §5-§10 — точечные заплатки В `infer_expr_c_type` (closure-return /
> tuple-of-closures / match-block-arm / sum-variant-disambig / same-name shadowing → ложный
> `nova_int`/`NovaOpt_nova_int` → CC-FAIL). Это РОВНО §0/§1-фрагментация, которую **U.4 убирает ПО
> ПОСТРОЕНИЮ** (codegen читает тип чекера, не re-derive). Используй §5-§10 как **acceptance/regression-
> корпус U.4** (когда codegen потребляет typed-IR — эти кейсы корректны конструкцией). **Отложенные
> маркеры закрываются U.4 (+ U.5.5c):** `[M-172-nova-int-fallback-audit]` (~78 сайтов, корневой класс);
> `[M-169.2-vec-fn-empty-literal-nova-int]` (явный инстанс); `[M-D215-defaults-handler-lambda-type]`
> (`Some(e)`→`NovaOpt_nova_int` без типа `e` из `Fail[E]` → нужен U.4 + **U.5.5c** effects-lossless —
> пересечение!). Сами заплатки §5-§10 — кандидаты на УДАЛЕНИЕ, когда корень уйдёт (проверять per-fix,
> не слепо). Подтверждает: 173/169-долги U.4 не переделывает, а ЧИНИТ.
>
> **M7 — инсайт: U.3.4 и U.4 — ОДНА труба.** «codegen потребляет резолюцию чекера» (U.3.4,
> resolved-callee по ExprId) и «codegen читает тип выражения» (U.4, resolved-type по ExprId) —
> один субстрат (ExprId → resolved-info в ModuleEnv → emitter). Строить совместно, не дублировать.
>
> **Уточнённая декомпозиция/порядок (с gated-реальностями):**
> - **U.4.1′ (substrate, landable сейчас):** `ExprId` (assign `Expr::new`, СОХРАНЯЕТСЯ при mono-клоне) +
>   `ModuleEnv.resolved_types: HashMap<ExprId,ResolvedType>` + провод как `set_proven_*` + продюсер-
>   литералы + equivalence-assert (annotation==legacy над корпусом). Закрывает keystone. Deps: none
>   (U.5 ✅ дал carrier). Перед коммитом дизайна — спайк (M4).
> - **U.4.2 (leaf/operator):** литералы/Binary/Unary/As читают аннотацию через новый `resolved_type_to_c`.
>   Deps: U.4.1′.
> - **U.3.4-prep (resolved-callee на том же субстрате):** чекер пишет выбранный overload (уже считает в
>   U.3.1/U.3.3). Разблокирует U.4.3. Deps: U.4.1′; гейт U.2.4 (mangling) для финальной замены
>   codegen-резолвера.
> - **U.4.3 (Call-арм, staged a/b/c/d):** только ПОСЛЕ U.3.4-prep; расщепление side-effect/type (M5);
>   multi-week. Deps: U.4.1′, U.4.2, U.3.4-prep.
> - **U.4.4 → U.4.5:** структурные армы (Member/Index/Match/…) → удаление legacy + thin shim. Deps: U.4.3, U.2.

> **РЕОРГ U.4 (2026-06-21) — единый канонический `ResolvedType` ([D315](../../spec/decisions/02-types.md#d315-resolvedtype--единый-канонический-носитель-типа-plan-1721-2026-06-21)).**
> Решением владельца зафиксирован принцип: `ResolvedType` — **ЕДИНОЕ каноническое окно правды о
> типе**; проверки / совместимость / конверсии / **перевод-в-C** выводятся из него; legacy
> `type_ref_to_c` (резолв+перевод в одном проходе — резолв-половина дублирует чекер, §0-анти-паттерн)
> **ретайрится**. Зафиксировано в [`compiler-conventions.md`](../compiler-conventions.md) §0/§10 + D315.
>
> **Отменяет M2.** Спайк 2026-06-21 (read-only, по коду ветки) доказал:
> - **Side-effects `type_ref_to_c` идемпотентны** (`register_novaopt_decl` guard `novaopt_decls_seen`;
>   worklist dup-guard `emitted_generic_type_instances`+`any(m==mangled)`; `register_mono_tuple`
>   set-insert) → в assert-режиме делегирование безопасно (legacy регистрирует ПЕРВЫМ, второй вызов —
>   no-op). Машинерия подавления эффектов НЕ нужна.
> - **Текущий `ResolvedType` ЛОССИ для C** (опровергает M2 «достаточен»): `from_type_ref` берёт
>   `path.last()` (теряет модуль → мис-мангл `Nova_Foo*` вместо `Nova_mymod_Foo*`); схлопывает
>   `*mut T`-форму `Pointer(Mut)` в `TypedPtr(Ro,…)` (теряет мутабельность → `const T*` вместо `T*`);
>   разворачивает L2 `readonly` (для C прозрачно, для ЧЕКА важно).
>
> **Подход «реконструировать `TypeRef` из `ResolvedType` на лоуэринге» ОТВЕРГНУТ** (D315): лосси
> round-trip = выбрасываемый костыль + возврат резолва-в-codegen (анти-§0). Вместо — **обогатить
> носитель до lossless-canonical и опускать его ОДНИМ `resolved_type_to_c`**.
>
> **Новая декомпозиция (порядок по deps):**
> - **U.5.5 — обогащение `ResolvedType` до lossless-canonical** (носитель — забота U.5). **(a) ✅ DONE
>   2026-06-21** (`6ba25a94` module-путь на `Named` / `9e27619a` `*mut`/`*unsafe`-верность / `99855cd0`
>   ось L2 `readonly` через `peel_view`): полная разрешённая идентичность (не `path.last()`) + верность
>   модификаторов указателя (`*mut`) + ось L2 `readonly` — ЛОКАЛЬНО, без name-res-зависимости, достаточно
>   для C-мангл-паритета; byte-identical конструкцией (несёт только `from_type_ref`, codegen его не зовёт,
>   `resolved_cat_of` view-прозрачен). **(b)** нормализация `Self`→приёмник и развёртка алиасов в момент
>   построения `ResolvedType` — нужна checker-name-res (soft-dep U.1.3/U.3), 📋 proposed.
>   **(c) effects LOSSLESS с type-args (`Fail[E]` несёт `E`) — ✅ DONE 2026-06-21** (`f7511bda`): был
>   `ResolvedType::Func.effects: Vec<String>` (только ИМЯ, `from_type_ref` брал `path.last()`, дропал
>   generics) → `Fail[E]` терял `E` → **лосси** (нарушение D315 «несёт ПОЛНУЮ семантическую личность»);
>   обогащён до **`Vec<ResolvedType>`** — каждый эффект = полный резолв (имя + module + args через
>   U.5.5(a)-lossless `Named`), `Fail[E]`/`Db[T]`/… несут type-args. Разблокирует typed-errors
>   [Plan 173](173-error-system-unify-harden.md) Ф.4 (`Fail[E]`-dispatch по `type_id`) + [Plan 175](175-any-type-and-is-downcast.md)
>   (`any`/`is`) — садятся на готовый носитель, не переделывая (umbrella 172 §3.1 п.1). **BYTE-IDENTICAL
>   КОНСТРУКЦИЕЙ:** `effects` — WRITE-ONLY (0 потребителей читают `ResolvedType::Func.effects`: codegen
>   `R::Func{..}`→`void*` игнорит; `cat_compatible_rt`/`distinct_mono` не рекурсируют в effects); единственная
>   конструкция — `from_type_ref`. Verify: multiset-.c=0 на 3 effects-heavy (patch+checkout); регресс 17/0;
>   unit `func_effects_carry_type_args_lossless`. Deps: U.5.1–U.5.4 ✅.
> - **U.4.6 — `resolved_type_to_c` до ПОЛНОГО паритета с `type_ref_to_c`** (ABI-лоуэринг в codegen:
>   мангл / Option / Result / generic-templates / value-records / protocols / tuple / array / erasure;
>   state-aware = финальная mono-подстановка + побочки эмиссии typedef'ов, но **БЕЗ резолва** — он
>   сделан чекером). Гейт: byte-identical vs `type_ref_to_c` над корпусом (`debug_assert` ДО
>   переключения каждого сайта). Deps: U.5.5.
> - **U.4.3 / U.4.4 (re-scope) — армы выражений ЧИТАЮТ аннотацию → `resolved_type_to_c`.** Резолв-несущие
>   армы (Call / Member / Index) дополнительно ждут канал «чекер→codegen: выбранный callee/field»
>   (U.3.4-prep, M3/M7) — не только перевод типа. Deps: U.4.6, U.3.4-prep.
>   - **U.4.4(ctor) ✅ DONE 2026-06-22 (`0790e375`)** — turbofish-ctor return (СИНТАКСИЧЕСКИЙ слайс,
>     byte-identical, см. §9). **U.4.4-prep.b (Member/Index/Ident — checker-channel) — РАЗВЕДКА+АУДИТ
>     2026-06-22, ОТКЛОНЁН как byte-identical-additive (находка, меняющая стратегию endgame):**
>     построен substrate (буфер в `TypeCheckCtx` + hook в `f1_expr` (центр. scope-walk) + lift + merge
>     в 2 пайплайнах), прогнан equivalence-assert на Ident (простейшая семант. арма — чекер уже выводит
>     scope-тип). **Assert ВСКРЫЛ: чекер-аннотация ≠ legacy `infer_expr_c_type`** — НЕ byte-identical
>     (в отличие от ctor). Detect-аудит (env-gated non-fatal, на ~150 фикстур): **21 событие, 2 класса:**
>     (1) `ok`: annot=`nova_bool` vs legacy=`nova_int` (15) — legacy падает в `_=>nova_int`-fallback (§1
>     анти-паттерн, ~78 сайтов), **чекер КОРРЕКТНЕЕ** = улучшение; (2) `x/v/item`: annot=`Nova_T*` vs
>     legacy=`void*` (6) — generic-T в erased-теле: аннотация generic-уровня `Nova_T*`, legacy стирает в
>     `void*` (lowering-context). **ВЫВОД:** byte-identical-prep (паттерн ctor/U.4.1/U.4.2: producer
>     write-only + consumer assert==legacy + release=legacy) **НЕ масштабируется** на семантические армы —
>     legacy интринзически багован (fallback'ы), поэтому чекер-аннотация их ФИКСИТ → flip = **behavior-change**,
>     не byte-identical. ⇒ **U.4.4/U.4.5 для семант. арм = behavior-change endgame** (gate generic-T класс +
>     flip consumer authoritative + **ПОЛНЫЙ регресс** §6.6, не сэмпл — output меняется, фиксит часть 17
>     leaks U.7.1). Дивергенция мала/ограничена (2 класса) → endgame трактуем, но это крупный risk-несущий
>     шаг (не инкрементальный byte-identical). Substrate-код + детект — throwaway, откатан. `[M-172.1-U4.4-semantic-arms-behavior-change]`.
> - **U.4.7 — миграция ОБЪЯВЛЕННЫХ типов** (сигнатуры / поля / возвраты) с `type_ref_to_c` на
>   «разрешить→опустить» (checker-resolve / `from_type_ref` → `resolved_type_to_c`). Это то, что делает
>   `resolved_type_to_c` способным заменить `type_ref_to_c` целиком. Deps: U.4.6.
> - **U.4.8 ✅ DONE 2026-06-21 (`e1f1d96a`) — удалить мёртвый `type_ref_to_c_impl`.** После U.4.7-флипа
>   `_impl` (~500 стр) достижим ТОЛЬКО для None-кейсов wrapper'а → свёрнут в `resolved_type_to_c`
>   (`Option<String>` → `Result<String,String>`: единый лоуэринг несёт Err сам — usize/isize/ptr removed,
>   Self-no-recv). `type_ref_to_c` стал тонким адаптером. Byte-identical (multiset-.c, ~55 дир). Полное
>   удаление адаптер-хопа `TypeRef→ResolvedType` на ~120 объявленных-тип сайтах = endgame U.6.1, OUT of
>   scope. Deps: U.4.7. (NB: армы выражений U.4.3/U.4.4/U.4.5 НЕ были блокером — `_impl` был мёртв уже после U.4.7.)
> - **U.4.5 (без изменений) — финальный флип legacy→IR + удаление дублей inference**; единый
>   full-corpus assert-прогон ПЕРЕД удалением (не per-арм флип сейчас).
>
> **U.4.1 ✅ / U.4.2 🟡 (§9) валидны как история** — примитивы lossless (literals / bool-ops / arith /
> prim-`As`). Их consumer = `legacy + assert` сохраняется до U.4.5. Реконструкция-костыль из
> прошлой разведки (Phase A «делегировать через реконструированный TypeRef») **не применяется** —
> заменён обогащением носителя (U.5.5).

#### U.4.1 — Add type-annotation side-table infrastructure (TypedIR substrate)
- **Что:** Introduce the substrate that lets a single semantic pass attach a resolved type to every Expr, so codegen can READ it instead of re-inferring. Production design (no shortcut): add an `ExprId`/stable-key mechanism (e.g. a per-fn-monotonic id assigned at parse or a `HashMap<Span, ResolvedType>` keyed by the already-unique Expr span — verify span uniqueness first) and a `ResolvedTypes` table living in ModuleEnv. Define a single canonical resolved-type carrier (reuse the U.5 structured type if U.5 lands first; otherwise carry `TypeRef`). Do NOT yet populate it for all exprs — only wire the plumbing + one trivial producer (literals) and one consumer-read path, both behind a feature-equivalence assert that the table value (when present) matches the legacy inference. This is the keystone: U.4 is impossible without a place to store annotations.
- **Где:** compiler-codegen/src/ast/mod.rs:1993 (Expr struct — decide span-key vs new id field; if id, thread through parser); compiler-codegen/src/types/mod.rs:62 (ModuleEnv — add `pub resolved_types` map) and ~7894 (infer_expr_type — emit annotations for literal arms first); a read accessor consumed at emit_c.rs:35718 (infer_expr_c_type entry — when annotation present and feature-flag on, assert-equal then return derived C-type).
- **Приёмка:** Production-grade, conforms to compiler-conventions.md §0/§1/§2. Positive: a literal expr (IntLit/StrLit/BoolLit) gets an annotation recorded by the semantic pass; codegen's infer_expr_c_type, when reading the annotation, derives an IDENTICAL C-string to the legacy path (debug-assert equality across the whole std+nova_tests corpus → 0 mismatches). Negative: a deliberately-wrong injected annotation makes the equivalence assert fire (test via a gated unit test). Span-key uniqueness proven by a corpus scan (0 collisions) OR id field threaded with a parser test. 0 regressions vs clean binary (full release nova test). Marker [M-172.1-U4-typedir-substrate] + backlog entry for the not-yet-annotated arms.
- **Blast-radius:** Adds a field/map; touches ModuleEnv (Debug/Default derive), parser if id-based. No behavior change while feature-flag off. Measure: `cargo build` clean; full `nova test` byte-identical C output with flag off (diff emitted .c). Risk surface = ModuleEnv consumers (codegen ctor reads env).
- **Deps:** none (but strongly prefer U.5.1-U.5.3 first so the carrier is the structured type, not TypeRef — see risk) · **Risk:** Span may NOT be unique across desugared/synthesized exprs (desugar.rs clones spans) → table collisions. De-risk: run a corpus scan counting duplicate spans per fn BEFORE choosing span-key; if collisions exist, use a threaded ExprId. This single decision gates all of U.4.

#### U.4.2 — Derive C-type strings from annotated IR for the leaf/literal/operator arms
- **Что:** Make codegen's infer_expr_c_type, for the arms that DON'T require resolution (IntLit, FloatLit, BoolLit, StrLit, CharLit, UnitLit, NullPtrLit, TupleLit, Binary, Unary, As, Block-trailing), READ the annotation produced by the semantic pass and lower it via a single `resolved_type_to_c` function, deleting the duplicated re-inference in those arms. The semantic pass (infer_expr_type) is extended to annotate exactly these arms. Keep the legacy code path live behind the equivalence assert until proven.
- **Где:** compiler-codegen/src/types/mod.rs:7894-8058 (extend infer_expr_type to annotate Binary/Unary/As/Block/Tuple — currently many return None); compiler-codegen/src/codegen/emit_c.rs:35793-35971 (replace literal+Binary+Unary+Block arms' re-inference with annotation read + resolved_type_to_c); new `resolved_type_to_c` next to type_ref_to_c:5769.
- **Приёмка:** Production-grade, conforms to §0/§1. For every leaf/operator expr in std+nova_tests, the C-type derived from the annotation equals the legacy infer_expr_c_type output (debug-assert, 0 mismatches over full corpus). Positive test: pointer-arith (`p - q`→int64_t), f64-wins, typed-int promotion (u32 ^ nova_int → u32) all still produce correct C. Negative: an annotation/legacy divergence is caught by the assert (gated unit test). Full release nova test 0 regressions vs clean binary; emitted .c diff empty for the touched arms.
- **Blast-radius:** Binary/Unary arms carry subtle promotion rules (pointer arith is_raw_cptr, typed-int-wins) — these MUST be reproduced in the semantic-pass annotation, else C output drifts → CC-FAIL. Measure: diff every emitted .c file before/after; expect 0 diff. ~10 arms, ~250 lines deleted from emit_c.rs.
- **Deps:** U.4.1 · **Risk:** Promotion semantics (typed-int vs nova_int, f64-wins, ptr-arith) are codegen-specific and not in the checker today → moving them risks output drift. De-risk: port the exact predicates (is_raw_cptr, is_typed_integer) into the semantic pass; assert-equal gate before deleting legacy.

#### U.4.3 — Move method/overload resolution result into the IR so the Call arm reads a resolved callee
- **Что:** This depends on U.3 (resolver in checker). Once the checker resolves each Call to a concrete callee + monomorphization, RECORD the callee's resolved return-type annotation in the IR table. Then make infer_expr_c_type's Call arm (the ~2000-line block) READ that annotation for the return type instead of re-running method_overloads/infer_mono_method_ret_with_args/resolve_overload. The codegen-only side-table machinery (var_types, generic_type_instance_info, mono-name decode) is retained ONLY for codegen's own emission (variable C-type tracking), not for type inference. Stage by Call shape: (a) free-fn calls, (b) static `Type.method`, (c) instance `obj.method`, (d) generic constructors — each its own commit.
- **Где:** compiler-codegen/src/codegen/emit_c.rs:36250-38287 (Call arm — replace return-type derivation with annotation read, sub-staged a/b/c/d); semantic pass call-resolution output (U.3 deliverable) feeding resolved_types; method_overloads:618 / resolve_overload:11140 become checker-owned (U.3), codegen consumes.
- **Приёмка:** Production-grade, conforms to §0/§1 (resolution lives in checker, codegen consumes). For each staged Call shape: C return-type from annotation == legacy over full corpus (0 mismatches). Positive: overloaded free-fn, generic Vec[T].with_capacity, str.* builtin, user instance method all get correct C type from IR. Negative: `no matching overload` is now a clean checker diagnostic (not codegen CODEGEN-FAIL) — EXPECT_COMPILE_ERROR fixture. 0 regressions vs clean binary; the deleted resolver code in emit_c.rs no longer reachable for type purposes.
- **Blast-radius:** LARGEST in U.4: ~2000 lines, 275 infer_expr_c_type call sites depend on Call-return correctness; coupled to mono-name string decoding and 5+ name-keyed override tables. Measure: full emitted-.c diff per stage; per-shape regression batch. Touching emit_c.rs hot region — coordinate.
- **Deps:** U.4.1, U.4.2, and U.3 (resolve_overload moved to checker) — HARD dependency · **Risk:** MULTI-WEEK by itself. The Call arm intertwines return-type inference with mono-instantiation registration side-effects (register_mono_tuple, lazy decl emission) — naively reading an annotation skips those side-effects → missing typedefs → CC-FAIL. De-risk: separate the SIDE-EFFECT registration (keep in codegen) from the TYPE derivation (move to IR read); stage a/b/c/d independently; do NOT attempt before U.3 is merged and stable.

#### U.4.4 — Collapse remaining structural arms (Member/Index/Ident/RecordLit/ArrayLit/Match) onto IR reads
- **Что:** Convert the remaining infer_expr_c_type arms (Ident:36044, Index:36084, Member, RecordLit:35972, ArrayLit:38287, Match) to read the IR annotation, with codegen retaining only the side-table reads it genuinely needs for emission (e.g. var C-type for declaration). Extend the semantic pass to annotate these arms (today infer_expr_type returns None for most). Delete the duplicated inference once each arm is assert-proven equal.
- **Где:** compiler-codegen/src/codegen/emit_c.rs:36044-38287 (Ident/Index/Member/RecordLit/ArrayLit/Match arms); compiler-codegen/src/types/mod.rs:7894 (annotate these in semantic pass — needs field/record-schema + array-element type knowledge from the unified registry U.2).
- **Приёмка:** Production-grade, §0/§1/§2 (no hardcoded stdlib; uses unified registry). For each arm: annotation-derived C-type == legacy over full corpus (0 mismatches). Positive: nested field-access chain element type, str[i]→char, Vec[u32] element decode, match-arm binding all correct. Negative: type errors surface as checker diagnostics not CC-FAIL. 0 regressions vs clean binary. After this task: infer_expr_c_type has NO independent resolution logic — it is a thin lowering of IR annotations.
- **Blast-radius:** Index/Member arms decode element types from mono C-names and consult last-wins folder-module side-tables (array_element_types poisoning, documented at emit_c.rs:36098) — moving inference to the checker must reproduce the AUTHORITATIVE element-type source (registry, not poisoned side-table). Measure: full .c diff. ~600 lines.
- **Deps:** U.4.3, U.2 (unified method/field registry) · **Risk:** Folder-module last-wins side-table poisoning is a known correctness hazard; the checker version must derive element types from the schema/registry, which is the RIGHT fix but expands scope. De-risk: rely on U.2's single registry; per-arm assert-equal gate; this arm-set is the natural place the U.4 goal ('infer_expr_c_type-resolution-logic disappears') is finally met.

#### U.4.5 — Delete legacy duplicate inference; flip codegen to IR-only; U.4 acceptance gate
- **Что:** Remove the now-dead legacy inference branches and the equivalence-assert scaffolding; make infer_expr_c_type a pure `resolved_type_to_c(ir.type_of(expr))` shim (or inline its few callers onto the IR accessor). Remove the checker's separate `infer_expr_type` Option<TypeRef> producer in favor of the single annotating pass (keep one function, one representation). Update docs + D-block (D312) noting single expression-inference source.
- **Где:** compiler-codegen/src/codegen/emit_c.rs:35718 (infer_expr_c_type → thin shim); compiler-codegen/src/types/mod.rs:7894 (infer_expr_type folded into the annotating pass, single source); docs/plans/172.1-unified-type-engine.md U.4 criterion; spec D312 + 09-tooling error-index for any diagnostics that moved.
- **Приёмка:** Production-grade, §0/§1. ONE expression-inference implementation remains (grep proves no second re-derive: infer_expr_c_type body has no resolution, only annotation read + lowering). Positive+negative corpus green via release nova; 0 regressions vs clean binary (full nova test). The equivalence asserts are removed only AFTER a full clean run with them ON shows 0 mismatches. docs/D312 updated; simplifications.md notes none introduced.
- **Blast-radius:** Final removal — if any arm was missed, CC-FAIL surfaces. Measure: full nova test + full emitted-.c diff vs clean binary must be empty. Closes [M-172.1-U4-typedir-substrate].
- **Deps:** U.4.2, U.4.3, U.4.4 · **Risk:** Removing the legacy path is irreversible-feeling; any un-migrated arm breaks. De-risk: keep asserts ON for one full green run before deletion; delete per-arm, not en masse.

> **РАЗВЕДКА U.5 (2026-06-20) — фактическое состояние width/sign-модели (сверено по коду).**
> Соответствие [`compiler-conventions.md`](../compiler-conventions.md) §0/§2.
>
> - **G1 — двойной int-collapse.** `Ty` (enum types/mod.rs:19) И `TyCat` (enum :8670) ОБА схлопывают
>   ВСЕ int-ширины в один вариант (`Ty::Int` / `TyCat::Int`) — width/sign теряются. `Ty` — `pub`, НО
>   cross-crate потребителей в compiler-codegen НЕТ (grep `types::Ty`/`types::TyCat` вне mod.rs — только
>   комменты/spec/docs). → U.5.4 может УДАЛИТЬ Ty/TyCat без facade (de-risk: проверить отд. крейт nova-lsp ДО удаления).
> - **G2 — width/sign восстанавливается ОТДЕЛЬНО, 3 standalone-fn (не методы).** `sized_int_bounds`:8557
>   (D227 literal range), `int_width_rank`:8603 (`(u8 width, bool signed)` из TypeRef, unwrap ro/mut/unsafe),
>   `is_int_narrowing`:8636 (narrowing-решение, поверх int_width_rank) + `sized_int_name`:8580, `lit_range_check`:8657.
>   Причина раздельности: `cat_compatible`:8689 PERMISSIVE на ширине (`(Int,Int)`→всегда true) → `is_int_narrowing`
>   нужен ОТДЕЛЬНЫМ вторым проходом поверх `assignable`:7765 (это и есть bolt-on, который U.5.2 сворачивает).
> - **G3 — оси L1/L2/L3 (D246/Plan147).** L2 view = `TypeRef::Readonly`/`Mut`; L3 pointee = `TypeRef::Pointer`
>   modifier → `Ty::TypedPtr(PointerModifier, Box<Ty>)`. `ty_of_ref`:13126 collapse-правила: `Readonly`→transparent;
>   `Mut`/`Unsafe(Pointer)`→TypedPtr; `Mut`/`Unsafe(non-ptr)`→transparent recurse (документированная асимметрия).
>   int-narrowing UNWRAP'ает ro/mut/unsafe (L2 transparent для int) — `from_type_ref` должен это сохранить byte-identical.
> - **G4 — конверсии-образцы.** `ty_of_ref`:13126 (TypeRef→Ty, 15 callers), `cat_of`/`cat_of_depth`:8362 (TypeRef→TyCat).
>   `from_type_ref` зеркалит их, но LOSSLESS для int (Scalar{width,signed} вместо collapse).
>
> **Уточнение декомпозиции:** U.5.1 (keystone) несёт width/sign (`Scalar`) + L3 (`TypedPtr`) как Ty; L2-view-обёртка
> — добавляется в U.5.2 ТОЛЬКО если rewire `assignable` потребует (сейчас assignable L2-transparent для int по D227/D54),
> иначе помечается `[M-172.1-U5-l2-view-deferred]` (не упрощение — соответствие текущей семантике unwrap). U.5.1 additive
> (как U.2.1): новый тип + `from_type_ref` + accessors + unit-тесты, БЕЗ rewire. Гейт U.5.2-U.5.4: assert new==old над
> корпусом ПЕРЕД удалением старого пути (раздельные is_int_narrowing/cat) + diagnostic-diff=0.

#### U.5.1 — Define the structured scalar type (width+sign+L1-L3 modifiers) as a single carrier
- **Что:** Introduce one structured type — e.g. `NScalar { width: IntWidth, signed: bool }` inside a broader `ResolvedType` enum that also carries L1 (binding mut) / L2 (content-view ro/mut) / L3 (pointee modifier) — replacing the lossy Ty/TyCat int-collapse. Define total constructors `from_type_ref(&TypeRef, &types) -> ResolvedType` (alias/newtype-resolving) and accessors `int_width_sign()`, `is_signed()`, `category()`. Do NOT yet rewire callers — land the type + conversions + exhaustive unit tests first. This is the U.5 keystone and the natural carrier for U.4.1.
- **Где:** compiler-codegen/src/types/mod.rs (new module/section near Ty:19 and TyCat:8653); conversions mirror ty_of_ref:13145 + cat_of_depth:8349 + int_width_rank:8586 but LOSSLESS for width/sign; unit tests asserting `int`≡i64=(64,signed), `uint`≡u64, u32=(32,unsigned), L1/L2/L3 preserved.
- **Приёмка:** Production-grade, §2 (only the documented primitive width/sign hardcode exception, with marker). Unit tests (cargo test): every primitive maps to the correct (width,sign); ro/mut/unsafe/pointer wrappers preserve L1/L2/L3; alias/newtype resolved via self.types. Negative: a non-int type returns the right non-scalar category (no panic). No behavior change yet (not wired). 0 regressions (it is additive). Marker [M-172.1-U5-structured-type] for the width/sign primitive hardcode (the sanctioned §2 exception, also covered by an existing D-block on int≡i64).
- **Blast-radius:** Additive only — new type + functions, no callers rewired. Measure: cargo build+test green; full nova test unchanged.
- **Deps:** none · **Risk:** Designing L1-L3 carriage to match the existing 3-axis mutability model (D246, Plan 147) — get it wrong and U.5.4 mis-enforces readonly. De-risk: mirror exactly the AST→Ty collapse rules at ty_of_ref:13209-13219 (Pointer/Mut/Unsafe → TypedPtr) and Plan 147 R2-split semantics; cite D246 in tests.

#### U.5.2 — Route assignability through the structured type; fold is_int_narrowing into it
- **Что:** Rewrite `assignable` (types/mod.rs:7748-7891) and `cat_compatible` to operate on the structured ResolvedType so the int-width/sign info is present IN the category decision, eliminating the bolted-on `is_int_narrowing(&found_tr, expected)` raw-TypeRef second pass (currently :7877-7885). Narrowing becomes a method on ResolvedType (`would_narrow_into(target)`), single source. sized_int_bounds/lit_range_check literal checks also consult the structured type. Keep diagnostics byte-identical (Compat::Narrowing/OutOfRange messages unchanged).
- **Где:** compiler-codegen/src/types/mod.rs:7748-7891 (assignable — replace cat_of+separate is_int_narrowing with one structured compare); :8619 is_int_narrowing → folded into ResolvedType method; :8672 cat_compatible → structured; :7769/7801 sized_int_name/lit_range_check consult structured type.
- **Приёмка:** Production-grade, §0/§1/§3 (no silent permissive without comment). Positive: widening (u8→int) OK, `as`-cast OK, identical-width OK. Negative: u32→i32, u64→int, signed→unsigned, narrowing arg all still fire [E_IMPLICIT_NARROWING]/[E7301] with the SAME message+span+code (EXPECT_COMPILE_ERROR fixtures unchanged). Literal range-check (D227) unchanged (300→u8 = OutOfRange). 0 regressions vs clean binary over full nova test; diagnostic snapshot diff empty. Removes the 'recover lost width' bolt-on noted in 172.1 U.5 criterion.
- **Blast-radius:** assignable is called from f1_check_call (call-arg checking), for-elem, let-binding (is_int_narrowing at :5398), reassignment — the core narrowing surface (~375 push(int) sites per Plan 172.2). Measure: full nova test diagnostic-count diff must be 0 (no new/lost errors); EXPECT_COMPILE_ERROR fixtures green.
- **Deps:** U.5.1 · **Risk:** Any difference in narrowing decision = false positive/negative across hundreds of sites. De-risk: keep the OLD is_int_narrowing live, assert new==old over full corpus before deleting; only then remove the raw-TypeRef pass.

#### U.5.3 — Fold the generic-arg-mismatch raw-TypeRef workaround into the structured type
- **Что:** Replace the raw-TypeRef generic_arg_mismatch second pass (f1_check_call:6562-6580, explicitly commented '[M-generic-arg-type-mismatch-silent] ... Ty/TyCat cannot') so the structured ResolvedType preserves generic type-arguments AND int width, letting the primary category compare catch `Vec[int]`→`Vec[u32]` directly — eliminating the bolt-on. concrete_primitive_name:13325 / generic_args:13297 / is_type_param_name:13313 either consume the structured type or are removed.
- **Где:** compiler-codegen/src/types/mod.rs:6562-6580 (the raw-TypeRef mismatch pass in f1_check_call Compat::Ok|Unknown arm); :8479 generic_arg_mismatch; :13297-13340 helpers; cat_of_depth:8386 Vec-arm (currently collapses element width) — structured type must NOT collapse.
- **Приёмка:** Production-grade, §0/§3. Positive: `Vec[int]`→`Vec[int]`, generic-param→anything stay OK (no false positive). Negative: `Vec[int]`→`Vec[u32]`, user `Stack[int]`→`Stack[u32]`, nested `Box[Option[int]]`→`Box[Option[u32]]` all flagged (same code+message+span as today; EXPECT_COMPILE_ERROR fixtures unchanged). 0 regressions vs clean binary. The marker [M-generic-arg-type-mismatch-silent] workaround is retired (folded into the unified compare); update marker/backlog.
- **Blast-radius:** Generic-arg mismatch fires on container element widths across std (codecs/buffers). Measure: full nova test diagnostic diff = 0; the existing generic-arg-mismatch fixtures green. cat_of_depth Vec-arm change affects all Array category comparisons.
- **Deps:** U.5.1, U.5.2 · **Risk:** The Vec-arm width-collapse was INTENTIONAL (comment at :8382) to avoid double-firing with the raw pass; un-collapsing must not now double-fire or change scalar-vs-generic distinction (scalar push(int) is NOT flagged, generic IS). De-risk: assert new==old over corpus; preserve the scalar-coercion-permitted / generic-distinct boundary exactly.

#### U.5.4 — Replace Ty/TyCat with the structured type across the checker; delete the three width helpers
- **Что:** Migrate all 46 TyCat / 28 Ty:: / 22 cat_of* usages in types/mod.rs to the structured ResolvedType, then DELETE the now-redundant Ty (or reduce to a thin alias), TyCat, cat_of/cat_of_depth/cat_compatible, and the three standalone width helpers (sized_int_bounds, int_width_rank — now methods). Keep Ty::Never semantics (bottom-type hook at assignable:7868) as a ResolvedType variant. ty_of_ref callers (15) migrated or shimmed.
- **Где:** compiler-codegen/src/types/mod.rs: Ty enum:19, ty_of_ref:13145 (+15 callers), TyCat:8653, cat_of_depth:8349, cat_compatible:8672, sized_int_bounds:8540, int_width_rank:8586 — all consolidated; Ty::Never hook at :7868 preserved as structured variant; any external Ty consumers (grep across crate).
- **Приёмка:** Production-grade, §0/§1. ONE width/sign/modifier representation (grep proves TyCat removed, cat_of* removed, int_width_rank/sized_int_bounds no longer standalone). Width/sign/L1-L3 available uniformly (172.1 U.5 criterion met). Positive+negative full corpus green via release nova; 0 regressions vs clean binary. Never-type assignability, ptr arithmetic ban, narrowing, range-check all preserved (existing fixtures green). D312 documents the single representation; simplifications.md notes none.
- **Blast-radius:** Widest U.5 task: 46+28+22 usage sites across the checker; Ty is pub (enum :19) — check cross-module/LSP consumers via grep before deleting. Measure: cargo build (no Ty/TyCat refs remain except sanctioned), full nova test 0 regressions, diagnostic diff 0.
- **Deps:** U.5.2, U.5.3 · **Risk:** Ty is `pub` and may be consumed by nova-lsp or other crates → deleting breaks them. De-risk: grep all crates for `types::Ty`/`TyCat` first; if external consumers exist, keep Ty as a thin facade over ResolvedType rather than deleting, and document. Do the migration mechanically arm-by-arm with full regression between batches (feedback-test-fix-per-file-loop).

### U.3 — Резолв перегрузок/методов + категориальная проверка в чекер (декомпозиция 2026-06-20)

> **Карта (Explore-обход, §7 шаг 1).** Чекерный `f1_check_call` (types/mod.rs:6792) резолвит вызов
> ТОЛЬКО при УНИКАЛЬНОМ overload (single candidate) — для free-fn (Ident) и non-primitive-receiver
> методов; при ≥2 или 0 кандидатах БЕЙЛИТ (`_ => return`: :6815 free-fn, :6847 Path-method, :6875
> module-qualified, :6899 instance-method) + **primitive-receiver guard :6843 ВСЕГДА бейлит** (str.from
> / int.method — арг-проверка пропущена; external overloads не в `fn_decls`). При уникальном кандидате
> args проверяются через `assignable` (категория lossless после U.5 + narrowing D54 + range D227 →
> E7301/E_IMPLICIT_NARROWING/E_LIT_OUT_OF_RANGE, :6920-6966). **Codegen-резолвер** (emit_c.rs:23036+,
> «D84»): выбирает overload по ТОЧНОМУ C-type-string match (:23043-52, без категориальной
> совместимости), ошибка «no matching overload» (:23057); self-method вариант :23159-73. **LEAK:**
> str↔int категориальное несовпадение для multi-overload / primitive-receiver вытекает в codegen/C
> (CC-FAIL), не ловится чекером. SigRegistry (`sig_registry.rs`) уже потребляется чекером (U.2.3,
> `build_base`/`lookup(receiver,name)→[SigEntry]`) — основа для arg-type резолва.

- **U.3.1** — Чекер резолвит free-fn overloads ПО ТИПАМ АРГУМЕНТОВ (через `SigRegistry.lookup`),
  убрать бейлы :6815/:6875; выбранный overload арг-проверить через `assignable`. **Detect-mode
  blast-radius ПЕРВЫМ** (сколько вызовов сейчас escape'ят чекер; сколько резолвятся уникально по
  arg-типу; сколько НОВО-зафайлятся как категория-mismatch). Deps: U.2.3 (✅).
- **U.3.2** — Закрыть primitive-receiver дыру :6843 (str.from(char) и т.п.). 🔴 **ГЕЙТНУТ на
  U.1/U.2/U.4** (карта 2026-06-20). Для primitive-receiver overload-набор **расщеплён**: `.nv`-методы
  → SigRegistry (чекер видит), а external (`str.from(char)`, StringBuilder/WriteBuffer/ReadBuffer)
  → **ExternalRegistry** — это «Plan 12: builtins.nv-driven hard-coded таблицы, embedded через
  `include_str!`» (external_registry.rs:1-3), которого у чекера НЕТ. Звучность U.3.x (checker-error ⊆
  codegen-error) требует, чтобы набор у чекера ⊇ codegen'овского; для primitive это сейчас НЕ так →
  правило дало бы false-positive. **Прибить ExternalRegistry к чекеру = §3-АНТИ-ПАТТЕРН** («ОДИН
  резолв питает чекер и codegen; никаких параллельных stdlib-реестров»). §3-корректный фикс:
  builtins.nv в ЕДИНЫЙ `.nv`-реестр (U.1/U.2), а он гейтнут на U.4 (`[M-172.1-U1-lib-import-needs-U4]`:
  инлайн lib-тел вскрывает codegen re-derive `infer_expr_c_type`). Поэтому U.3.2 — ПОСЛЕ U.1/U.2/U.4,
  НЕ хаком сейчас. Deps: U.1, U.2, U.4.
- **U.3.3** — ✅ DONE (`d02a06ab`, 2026-06-20) для **non-primitive Path-методов** (`Type.method`, :6847):
  та же arity-aware `overload_applicability`, что U.3.1; method params исключают receiver →
  выравнивание 1:1 с args. Гейт: detect172 pos (single/multi-param/арность)+neg; корпус
  protocols(MyNum.from)/plan108_1/plan126(StringBuilder.from) 0 нового кода; lib 868/5. **Остаток:**
  instance-методы `obj.method` (:6899, receiver-type inference) — **✅ DONE `f3ba0013` 2026-06-21**
  (см. §9-строку U.3.3-instance): `check_instance_overload` в Member-арме `f1_check_call`, recv-тип
  через self-less `BoundCtx::infer_arg_ty`, та же permissive arity-aware логика; primitive-recv gated
  (U.3.2). §7-замер: 0 WOULD-FLAG на 707K вызовов. Deps: U.3.1.
- **U.3.4** — Codegen ПОТРЕБЛЯЕТ резолюцию чекера (убрать D84-резолвер emit_c.rs:23036+ / он доверяет
  чекеру). **ГЕЙТ на U.2.4** (mangling-унификация `[M-172.1-U2.4-mangling-fragmented]`) + carrier
  резолюции (typed IR, U.4). Deps: U.2.4, U.4.
- **U.3.5** — str↔int категория = чекерная диагностика (вытекает из U.3.1-3); reclassify
  `EXPECT_CC_ERROR` type-class → CODEGEN-FAIL (связь с U.7.1). Deps: U.3.1-3.

> **Риск/природа.** U.3.1-3 — ADDITIVE-СТРОЖЕ (чекер начинает ловить то, что молча уходило в C) →
> **НЕ byte-identical** (это и есть цель §0/§1), вскроют молчавшие ошибки в std/nova_tests →
> blast-radius + миграция зависимостей В ТОМ ЖЕ шаге (§7 шаг 4). Поэтому КАЖДЫЙ — detect-mode
> (non-fatal count newly-errors над полным корпусом) ПЕРЕД включением fatal; калибровка на ноль
> ложных срабатываний (permissive на generic/alias/unknown). U.3.4 (удаление codegen-резолвера) —
> отдельно, гейт на U.2.4+U.4. Plan 172.2 (`vec_u32.push(int)`) — узкий первый срез U.3.1-3.

> **РЕЗУЛЬТАТ U.3.1 de-risk — blast-radius (detect-mode, non-fatal счётчики бейлов `f1_check_call`,
> 50 dirs, 2026-06-20).** Инструментированы 4 бейл-точки; уникальные (site,callee) записи:
> - **`freefn_multi` = 7 fn** (ЦЕЛЬ U.3.1, free-fn с ≥2 overloads, чекер их НЕ резолвит по arg-типу):
>   `assert`, `debug_assert`, `panic` (prelude) + `p139_make_str`/`p139_str_byte_sum`/`p139_cstr_strlen`/
>   `sum_range` (тестовые). **Магнитуда — единицы → миграция крошечная, U.3.1 viable.**
> - `method_multi` = 2 (`StringBuilder.from`, `MyNum.from`) → U.3.3.
> - `prim_recv` = 20 (str/int-методы, всегда бейлят) → U.3.2.
> - `freefn_unknown` = 74, `method_unknown` = 65 — **НЕ overload-цели**: callee вне `fn_decls` чекера
>   (builtins/intrinsics/cross-module-not-merged) — резолв уникальности неприменим, отдельный класс.
>
> **Следующий шаг U.3.1 (impl):** резолвить free-fn overloads по типам аргументов через
> `SigRegistry.lookup` в чекере, арг-проверить выбранный через `assignable`; калибровка на ~7 fn
> (особо `panic`/`assert` — format/variadic-перегрузки: НЕ словить false-positive). Detect-mode
> (count newly-errors) перед fatal. Instrumentation — throwaway (`detect_u3.rs`), откатана после замера.

> **РЕЗУЛЬТАТ U.3.1 — ✅ IMPLEMENTED (2026-06-20), `87e2bc05` + фикс `32b985ab`.** Чекер резолвит
> free-fn overloads: helper `overload_applicability -> Option<bool>` (None = не bind'ится по арности;
> Some(false) = bind+Bad-арг; Some(true) = bind+ок; permissive на Narrowing/OutOfRange/Unknown/Ok —
> codegen делает финальную exact-C-type селекцию, U.3.4); ветка `Some(multi)` эмитит
> **`[E_NO_MATCHING_OVERLOAD]`** ТОЛЬКО когда ≥1 overload bind'ится по арности, но НИ ОДИН не совместим
> по типу.
> **⚠ БАГ В ПЕРВОЙ ВЕРСИИ (`87e2bc05`) + ФИКС (`32b985ab`):** первый helper считал arity-несовпадение
> (bind fail) «type-несовместимостью» → 0-arg/wrong-arity ссылка на multi-overload free-fn давала
> **false-positive** `E_NO_MATCHING_OVERLOAD`. Мой тезис «звучен по построению (checker-error ⊆
> codegen-error)» оказался **НЕПОЛНЫМ** — он покрывал только Bad-арг, но не arity-mismatch (где helper
> тоже возвращал false). **Корпус ~78 dirs + аргумент-построения ЭТО ПРОПУСТИЛИ** (нет такой формы среди
> assert/panic/p139_*). Поймал **multi-param/arity тест в detect172/u3_1** (по запросу владельца — урок:
> тестировать тщательно в detect172, не полагаться на корпус/умозрительную звучность). Фикс: arity-aware
> (arity-mismatch — отдельный класс, репортит BoundCtx). Уточнённая звучность: для arity-применимых
> overload'ов Bad-арг ⟹ C-типы не совпадут ⟹ codegen тоже не нашёл бы match.
> **ГЕЙТ (behavior-change, не byte-identical):**
> (1) `detect172/u3_1/` pos+neg по test-conventions.md (pos: single/variable/MULTI-param/арность, тест-блок
> на сценарий; neg: `_neg`-суффикс, без test-блока, single + multiparam) — санкционированный дом тестов;
> (2) монотонность (ветка только ДОБАВЛЯет код ошибки); (3) arity-aware звучность.
> **`nova_tests` НЕ гейт** (сломан, per §6 — только byte-identical baseline): supporting-выборка ~78 dirs
> подтвердила 0 `E_NO_MATCHING_OVERLOAD` на позитиве. Проверено: в `nova_tests` НЕТ neg-фикстуры на free-fn
> overload (единственная overload-фикстура `plan65/.../f12_a_ts_minus_mono_neg` — method `@minus`, т.е.
> U.3.3-territory, U.3.1 её не трогает). lib 868/5 pre-existing. **НЕ byte-identical** (additive-строже —
> цель §0/§1). `E_NO_MATCHING_OVERLOAD` → в D312
> (консолидированный D-блок 172.1 на закрытие umbrella). U.3.2/U.3.3 (primitive-recv :6843 + method
> overloads :6847/:6899) — тем же приёмом, следующие. U.3.4 (удалить codegen-резолвер) — гейт U.2.4+U.4.

### U.6+U.7 — Свернуть дубли + C не ловит типы

> **Summary.** U.6 ("свернуть дубли codegen") collapses the type→C lowering and overload-signature helpers that the codegen layer reimplements 2-4× into single shared functions, and de-duplicates the const-fn pipeline's standalone TypeRef-unification engine. Current state: (1) THREE TypeRef→C-string mappings drift independently — `type_ref_to_c` (emit_c.rs:5769, the full one with mono-subst + Option/Result/protocol arms), `simple_type_ref_to_c` (emit_c.rs:14752, a static lossy mirror, called only from itself + the turbofish-member inference at emit_c.rs:36280), and `apply_type_subst_to_ref` (emit_c.rs:14590, primitive-only subst variant returning Option<String>); all three carry hand-copied primitive tables that already drifted (u32/u16 were missing → Vec[u32] mis-mangled, fixed in Plan 152.8). (2) `sum_schema_registry` (codegen/sum_schema_registry.rs) is now READ at ~30 sites in emit_c.rs (find_variant_compat/lookup_sum_schema/lookup_method_routing) but the legacy `sum_schemas: HashMap` field (emit_c.rs:596, ~117 references) is STILL the authoritative variant-layout/field-c-type store — the registry sits parallel and only `init_hardcoded_baseline().method_routing` is reclassified as legitimate runtime-registry (simplifications.md:10737). (3) `typeref_sig`/`param_sig`/`approx_arg_sig_lit`/`overload_compatible` are byte-for-byte duplicated between codegen/may_gc.rs (:154/:143/:208/:222) and codegen/preempt_keep.rs (:103/:91/:140/:156) — comments literally say "Identical to preempt_keep::…". (4) The const-fn pipeline (const_fn_trampoline.rs) is a standalone unification engine: `unify_type` (:1074), `type_refs_eq` (:1140), `subst_type_ref` (:1186), `infer_generic_subst` (:1027), `build_fn_signature_registry` (:1001) — the checker has only `typeref_equal` (types/mod.rs:13238, structural eq, no generic unification) and no shared unify, so this engine genuinely re-implements substitution/unification that nothing else exposes.  U.7 ("C не ловит типы") is the umbrella's guarantee gate: a permanent test-suite + harness assertion that on a CORRECT frontend zero positive-corpus tests end in CC-FAIL for type reasons, and that intentionally-wrong-type fixtures produce clean Nova CODEGEN-FAIL diagnostics, never the `Stage::Cc → "CC-FAIL"` outcome (test_runner.rs:1604). The runner already distinguishes stages (Stage::Codegen→"CODEGEN-FAIL", Stage::Cc→"CC-FAIL") and supports an `EXPECT_CC_ERROR` marker (test_runner.rs:165) used by capability-isolation tests — U.7 inverts that: it must AUDIT existing EXPECT_CC_ERROR uses, reclassify type-class ones as front-end gaps, and add a positive guarantee.

RECOMMENDED ORDER OF ALL PHASES U.1..U.7 (and 172.2 prerequisites): The hard dependency chain is U.1 → U.2 → U.3, which the plan correctly states. U.1 (checker reads ExternalRegistry instead of the hardcoded `builtins: HashSet`) unblocks everything because it gives the checker stdlib signatures. U.2 (one method/signature registry consumed by both layers) depends on U.1. U.3 (move overload/method resolution + D84 into the checker, removing f1_check_call's `_ => return` at :6476) depends on U.2. **Plan 172.2 (method-arg type-checking) is the first concrete slice of U.1-U.3 on the narrow `vec_u32.push(int)` case and is gated on at least U.1 (checker must see builtin `Vec.push` signature); doing full 172.2 cleanly wants U.2/U.3 too, but 172.2 can ship a narrow version after U.1 alone.** U.4 (single expression inference) and U.5 (single width/modifier representation) are consolidation that should follow U.3 because they assume resolution already lives in the checker. **U.6 is LARGELY INDEPENDENT of U.1-U.5: it is pure codegen-internal de-duplication and can run in PARALLEL / EARLY as low-risk churn-reduction** — in fact the U.6 helper-consolidation (especially U.6.3 typeref_sig and U.6.1 type→C merge) is best done EARLY so that U.4/U.5 inherit one lowering function instead of three. The only U.6 sub-task that genuinely depends on later phases is U.6.4 (const-fn engine over the shared one), which is most cleanly finished once U.4/U.5 give a shared unification/width representation; before that it can only be partially consolidated (extract a single `unify_type`/`subst_type_ref` into a shared module). U.7 is the FINAL gate and depends on all prior phases having removed the type-class CC-FAILs (especially U.3, which converts the `no matching overload` and category-mismatch failures into checker diagnostics); U.7's audit/harness scaffolding (U.7.1) can and should be built EARLY to measure the baseline, but the zero-CC-FAIL guarantee (U.7.3) can only be asserted green after U.3/U.4. Net recommended order: **U.6.3 → U.6.1 → U.6.2 (early, low-risk) ‖ U.1 → U.2 → U.3 (→ Plan 172.2) → U.4 → U.5 → U.6.4 → U.7**.
>
> **Feasibility.** Realistically completable as production-grade, but with two honest caveats. (1) U.6 is mostly low-to-medium-risk codegen-internal de-dup and is achievable now, EXCEPT two tasks: U.6.2.b (sum_schemas→registry read migration) is HIGH risk because sum-layout drift is silent (mis-compiled pattern matching) — it must be done in detect-mode (debug_assert legacy==registry over a full corpus run) before switching, and it should NOT be attempted without the U.6.2.a audit gate; and U.6.4.a only EXTRACTS/shares the const-fn unification engine — the plan's literal goal 'const-fn engine over the shared one' (i.e. const-fn substitution routed through the SAME engine codegen mono uses) is NOT fully achievable until U.4/U.5 deliver a shared expression-inference + width representation, so I split out the achievable extraction and explicitly deferred the full unification behind `[M-172.1-U6-constfn-unified]`. Attempting full const-fn-over-unified-IR now would be a multi-week effort entangled with U.4/U.5 and should be gated on them. (2) U.7's zero-CC-FAIL GUARANTEE (U.7.3 with an empty allowlist) is NOT achievable within U.6/U.7 alone — it structurally depends on U.3 (overload/category resolution moved to the checker) and Plan 172.2 (method-arg narrowing) to convert the remaining type-class CC-FAILs into checker diagnostics. Therefore U.7 is correctly scoped here as: build the harness + negative suite + gate NOW (green with a marker-cited known-gaps allowlist), and the allowlist shrinks to empty as U.3/U.4/172.2 land. This is the right decomposition — U.7's infrastructure is buildable and valuable immediately (it measures the baseline and prevents NEW leaks), while its terminal guarantee is a cross-phase outcome, not a single-phase deliverable. No single task above is a multi-week effort on its own given this split; U.6.2.b and U.6.4.a are the two that most need the detect-mode/deferral discipline called out in their risk notes.
>
> **Критерий приёмки фазы.** U.6 done when: (1) there is exactly ONE TypeRef→C primitive mapping shared by type_ref_to_c, apply_type_subst_to_ref (and the deleted simple_type_ref_to_c's former caller) — no third/fourth drift-prone primitive table (resolves the recurring Vec[u32]-style mis-mangle class at its root); (2) the overload-signature helpers (typeref_sig/param_sig/approx_arg_sig_lit/overload_compatible) exist once and are consumed by both may_gc.rs and preempt_keep.rs (the 'Identical to…' comments are eliminated by actual sharing); (3) declared-sum variant-existence + field-layout READS go through sum_schema_registry as the single read path (bucket a/b migrated), with mono'd-key paths explicitly marked as tracked gaps; (4) the const-fn TypeRef structural-eq + substitution + unification helpers live in one shared module consumed by both the const-fn pipeline and the checker's typeref_equal, with full 'const-fn over the unified IR' deferred behind a documented `[M-*]`. Every U.6 task: production-grade (no `#[allow(dead_code)]`/stub left, both old copies removed), conforms to compiler-conventions.md §0 (single source of truth), §2 (no new hardcoded type tables), §9 (no duplicated type resolution); each verified by positive tests (existing regress-guard fixtures compile+run unchanged) AND negative tests (a deliberate divergence in the shared helper visibly changes both consumers / a reverted de-dup re-introduces a CC-FAIL caught by U.7); 0 regressions vs a CLEAN binary (git stash + rebuild per §6.5) on the full `nova test` for layout-sensitive groups (sum/pattern/generic/const-fn), not a sample.  U.7 done when: a permanent harness reports zero NEW un-expected type-class CC-FAILs on the positive corpus and the intentionally-wrong-type negative suite yields clean Nova CODEGEN-FAIL diagnostics (never Stage::Cc), enforced as a gating CI check with a shrinking, marker-cited known-gaps allowlist (empty only after U.3/U.4/172.2 land). Every U.7 fixture is positive+negative via RELEASE nova in neg/ folder-modules per test-conventions.md §7, with each not-yet-enforced class carrying a `[M-172.1-U7-*]` marker + backlog entry per §3 (no silent holes). All observable new codes/markers reflected in spec error-index (§4); D312 updated.

#### U.6.3.a — Extract shared overload-signature helpers into one module
- **Что:** Create a new sibling module (e.g. codegen/overload_sig.rs) holding ONE copy each of `typeref_sig`, `param_sig`, `approx_arg_sig_lit`, and `overload_compatible`, made `pub(crate)`. These four are byte-for-byte duplicated today (comments in both files literally say 'Identical to preempt_keep::…'). Replace the private copies in may_gc.rs and preempt_keep.rs with `use` of the shared versions. Preserve EXACT current behavior (the may_gc and preempt_keep copies are confirmed identical, including the `?`/`<` permissive arms). Do NOT change any logic — this is a pure move/de-dup.
- **Где:** NEW codegen/overload_sig.rs (register in codegen/mod.rs:1-8); remove definitions at codegen/may_gc.rs:143 (param_sig), :154 (typeref_sig), :208 (approx_arg_sig_lit), :222 (overload_compatible) and codegen/preempt_keep.rs:91, :103, :140, :156; replace with `use crate::codegen::overload_sig::{...}` at top of each file.
- **Приёмка:** Positive: `cargo build --release` clean; `cargo test -p compiler-codegen` green (may_gc/preempt_keep unit tests unchanged). Negative: a deliberate divergence (temporarily edit the shared `typeref_sig` to render `f32` as `?`) must visibly change BOTH may_gc and preempt_keep behavior via a unit test that asserts the shared fn output — proving single source. Regress: full `nova test` sample (~1500) byte-identical pass/fail counts vs clean binary (these helpers only affect may-GC/preempt edge classification, which must not change generated C). Conforms to compiler-conventions.md §9 (no resolver duplication). Production-grade: no `#[allow(dead_code)]` left, both old copies fully removed.
- **Blast-radius:** may_gc/preempt_keep drive may-GC and preempt-keep call-graph flags → wrong output would change which fns get GC-safepoints. Measure: diff generated `.c` for a 50-file sample before/after — must be byte-identical. No std/nova_tests behavior site changes expected (pure internal helper move).
- **Deps:** none · **Risk:** Low. Risk: the two copies are NOT actually identical in some subtle arm. De-risk: do a literal text diff of the four fn bodies across both files BEFORE moving; if any arm differs, STOP and treat as a real merge (document which behavior is canonical) rather than assuming identity.

#### U.6.1.a — Make simple_type_ref_to_c delegate to type_ref_to_c (eliminate the static lossy mirror)
- **Что:** `simple_type_ref_to_c` (emit_c.rs:14752) is a `static` lossy duplicate of `type_ref_to_c` (emit_c.rs:5769) that already drifted (u32/u16 missing → Vec[u32] mis-mangle, Plan 152.8). Its ONLY non-test caller is the turbofish-member inference at emit_c.rs:36280 (and its own recursion). Convert that one call site to use the instance method `type_ref_to_c` (which already handles current_type_subst, Option/Result canonical mangling, protocols, aliases). The site at 36280 already special-cases type-params via current_type_subst before falling to simple_type_ref_to_c, so wiring `self.type_ref_to_c` there is straightforward. Then DELETE `simple_type_ref_to_c`. This removes one of the three drift-prone primitive tables.
- **Где:** emit_c.rs:36264-36283 (turbofish-member type_args_c map closure — replace `Self::simple_type_ref_to_c(tr)` with `self.type_ref_to_c(tr).unwrap_or_else(...)`); delete fn body emit_c.rs:14752-14811; verify no other references remain (Grep `simple_type_ref_to_c`).
- **Приёмка:** Positive: `Vec[u32].new()`, `HashMap[str,int].new()`, `Vec[Option[int]].new()` turbofish-member chains still compile and run (regress-guard fixtures from Plan 152.8 + 131 must pass). Negative: none new (no new rule). Conforms §0/§2 (single type→C path). Production-grade: fn fully deleted, no static helper left. Regress: 0 delta vs clean binary on full `nova test` sample; specifically the [M-154.1-chained-vec-f32-method-misdispatch] and Vec[u32] fixtures byte-identical C.
- **Blast-radius:** Only the turbofish-member inference path (HashMap[K,V].new() / Vec[T].new() chains). Measure: build the prelude + std/collections + any test using `Type[..].method()` turbofish; diff generated C names (must stay e.g. `Nova_Vec____uint32_t`). Risk if `type_ref_to_c` returns a trailing `*` where simple_type_ref_to_c did not — verify the mangle output equivalence on a Vec[u32] / Vec[Option[int]] sample before deleting.
- **Deps:** none · **Risk:** Medium. type_ref_to_c is instance-method (needs &self) and richer; at the 36280 site `self` is available. Risk: type_ref_to_c's alias/protocol arms could resolve a type-param name differently than the lossy mirror. De-risk: the call site already resolves type-params via current_type_subst FIRST (36274-36278); keep that guard, only the fallback changes. Detect-mode: temporarily assert_eq!(old, new) at the site over a corpus run before deleting.

#### U.6.1.b — Fold apply_type_subst_to_ref primitive table into type_ref_to_c's primitive resolver
- **Что:** `apply_type_subst_to_ref` (emit_c.rs:14590) carries a THIRD hand-copied primitive→C table (int/i64/uint/u64/f64/f32/bool/str/u8/u32/u16/i8/i16/i32/char) that already drifted (u32 etc. fixed in Plan 152.8). Extract the primitive-name→C-string mapping from `type_ref_to_c` into a single private helper `fn primitive_name_to_c(name:&str)->Option<&'static str>` and have BOTH `type_ref_to_c` (the Named/empty-generics arm) and `apply_type_subst_to_ref` call it. `apply_type_subst_to_ref` keeps its distinct subst-lookup + Option<String> contract (it cannot resolve user types without the registry — documented), but the primitive table is no longer a separate copy. This removes the last drift-prone duplicated primitive list.
- **Где:** emit_c.rs:5788-5824 (type_ref_to_c primitive match arms → call new helper) and emit_c.rs:14605-14627 (apply_type_subst_to_ref `match name.as_str()` → call same helper); NEW private `primitive_name_to_c` near type_ref_to_c.
- **Приёмка:** Positive: all fixed-width-int container fixtures (Vec[u32]/Vec[u16]/Vec[i32], Plan 152.8) compile + run; usize/isize still error with the Plan 133 messages (those are in type_ref_to_c's arm, not the primitive helper — keep them where they Err). Negative: `usize` field still `EXPECT_COMPILE_ERROR type \`usize\` is removed`. Conforms §2 (one width table). Production-grade: exactly one primitive table; the two callers share it. Regress: 0 delta vs clean binary, full sample.
- **Blast-radius:** Every mono'd generic instance name + every param/return C-type goes through these two functions. Measure: diff generated C for a broad sample (prelude+collections+numerics tests) — mangled names must be byte-identical. The `never`→nova_int and `u8`→nova_byte aliasing must be preserved exactly (Option[byte]≠Option[u8] mangle distinction, Plan 70.4).
- **Deps:** none · **Risk:** Medium. type_ref_to_c returns Result (with Err arms for usize/isize/ptr) while apply_type_subst_to_ref returns Option and falls through to None for non-primitives. De-risk: the new helper returns ONLY the pure primitive mapping (Some/None); the usize/isize/ptr Err arms stay in type_ref_to_c. Verify byte-identical mangle on a Vec[u32]/Option[byte]/Option[u8] corpus before/after.

#### U.6.2.a — Audit + document the sum_schemas vs sum_schema_registry boundary (de-risk gate, no behavior change)
- **Что:** Before collapsing, precisely map which data each store owns. Legacy `sum_schemas: HashMap<sum,HashMap<variant,Vec<field_c_type>>>` (emit_c.rs:596) is the AUTHORITATIVE field-layout store (~117 refs). `sum_schema_registry` (SumSchemaRegistry) is READ at ~30 sites (find_variant_compat / lookup_sum_schema / lookup_method_routing) and its `init_hardcoded_baseline().method_routing` is reclassified as legitimate runtime-registry (simplifications.md:10737, NOT to be deleted). Produce a written inventory (in the plan/backlog, NOT a stray .md): for each of the ~117 `sum_schemas` accesses, classify as (a) variant-existence lookup → already covered by registry.find_variant_compat, (b) field-c-type layout read → registry has field_c_types and could cover, (c) mono'd-key special path (e.g. emit_c.rs:12999/13126) → needs registry mono support first. Output: the count in each bucket + which sites are mechanically migratable now vs blocked.
- **Где:** Read sites: emit_c.rs:596 (field decl), and the ~117 `sum_schemas` accesses (e.g. :9978, :10017, :10225, :12966-13011, :13126, :15861); registry API: sum_schema_registry.rs:216 (lookup_sum_schema), :888 (find_variant_compat), :238 (find_variant_v2). No code change.
- **Приёмка:** Positive: an inventory table (in docs/plans/172.1 or backlog-followups.md) classifying every `sum_schemas` read site into buckets a/b/c with counts; explicit list of mechanically-migratable sites. Negative: n/a (audit). Conforms §6 (map before edit) and §3 (gaps documented with markers). Production-grade: the audit is exhaustive (count matches Grep total), not sampled.
- **Blast-radius:** None (no code change). This task EXISTS to bound the blast radius of U.6.2.b.
- **Deps:** none · **Risk:** Low. Risk: under-counting mono'd-key paths leads U.6.2.b to break Result/Option mono. De-risk: explicitly enumerate every site that keys `sum_schemas` by a name containing `____` (mono'd) — those are bucket c.

> **РЕЗУЛЬТАТ U.6.2.a — инвентаризация `sum_schemas` (audit 2026-06-20, без правки кода).**
> Exhaustive grep: **58** рефов `sum_schemas` в `emit_c.rs` (план переоценивал «~117»; фактически 58). Поле — `sum_schemas: HashMap<String, HashMap<String, Vec<String>>>` (sum-name → variant-name → Vec<field_c_type>), `emit_c.rs:573`.
>
> **Bucket-разбивка по 58 рефам:**
> - **WRITES / population (9):** ctor `:1307` + inserts `:2242` (MemOrdering), `:2893` (sync-types), `:10007`, `:10075` (empty), `:10215`, `:10756` (empty), `:10885`, `:15747`. Registry зеркалит их через `register_user_sum` (Phase-1 invariant). НЕ read-цель; writes мигрируют ПОСЛЕДНИМИ (после всех reads).
> - **Bucket (a) — type/variant EXISTENCE (19 `contains_key`):** is-known-concrete-type `:5848 :6178 :12267 :12604 :12630 :16789 :27595 :32081 :32435 :35415 :35474 :37726 :38152`; write-guard (existence-before-insert) `:2229 :2868 :9968`; eff_key-selection `:19924 :19926`; opt_eq guard `:12923`. → `registry.lookup_sum_schema(name).is_some()`. **Замечание:** 13 из них в OR-цепочке с `record_schemas` + `generic_types` («известный конкретный тип») — мигрируется только sum-половина, цепочка сохраняется.
> - **Bucket (b) — field-c-type LAYOUT reads (6):** `:12926` (emit_field_eq структурный `==`), `:19932-34` (pattern field-types), `:30042-43` (pattern-bind field-types), `:32172-74` (pattern field-types), `:33581-82` (find_variant — итерация по ВСЕМ sum'ам). → `registry.lookup_sum_schema().variants[].field_c_types` / `find_variant_compat`.
> - **Bucket (c) — mono'd-реконструкция (BLOCKED, 1 хелпер + 1 caller):** `build_mono_sum_schema` `:13083` читает GENERIC-базу (НЕ mono'd-ключ) + его caller — emit_field_eq mono-fallback `:12956-12969`. **Прямых mono'd-key (`____`) доступов — 0** (план опасался «:12999/:13126»): mono-обработка ЦЕНТРАЛИЗОВАНА в `build_mono_sum_schema`, который реконструирует mono'd-схему из generic-базы + записанных type-args (legacy-ключ — generic-имя, не mono'd). Registry МОГ БЫ покрыть (у него есть generic-base entry), но это самый рискованный путь → `[M-172.1-U6-sumschema-mono]`, defer.
>
> **Итог миграбельности:** **25 read-сайтов мигрируемы СЕЙЧАС** (19 existence + 6 field-layout, ключи стабильные generic/non-mono); **2 заблокированы** (bucket-c mono-реконструкция); 9 writes — последними.
>
> **Главный де-риск для U.6.2.b (ОБЯЗАТЕЛЬНО):** registry использует **precedence** `Prelude>User>Baseline` (`SchemaSource`, sorted DESC), а legacy `sum_schemas` — **last-write-wins** (HashMap insert). На same-name коллизии (prelude+user одно имя) они МОГУТ разойтись. → detect-режим `debug_assert!(legacy_result == registry_result)` над ПОЛНЫМ корпусом ПЕРЕД переключением КАЖДОГО read; только при 0 mismatch — switch. Это калибрует precedence↔last-write эквивалентность.

#### U.6.2.b — Migrate variant-existence + field-layout reads from legacy sum_schemas to sum_schema_registry (bucket a/b only)
- **Что:** Per the U.6.2.a inventory, mechanically replace bucket-a (variant existence) and bucket-b (field-c-type layout) `sum_schemas.get(...)`/`.contains_key(...)` reads with the registry equivalents (find_variant_compat / lookup_sum_schema + field_c_types), so the registry becomes the single read path for declared sum-layout. Leave bucket-c (mono'd-key special paths) on legacy until U.4/U.5 give the registry mono support — mark those with `[M-172.1-U6-sumschema-mono]` + backlog entry. Keep `sum_schemas` POPULATION as-is (registry already mirrors it via register_user_sum); this task only redirects READS, so the writes can be removed in a later step once all reads are migrated.
- **Где:** The bucket-a/b sites identified in U.6.2.a, e.g. existence checks at emit_c.rs:6188, :12310, :16903; layout reads at :12966-13011. Use sum_schema_registry.rs:216/:888 APIs.
- **Приёмка:** Positive: pattern-matching, @equal/@compare for sum types, Option/Result construction all still compile + run (regress-guard: plan 62.A.bis + 59 + 131 fixtures). Negative: malformed variant still produces the SAME diagnostic as before (no new error class). Conforms §0 (single source for sum-layout reads). Production-grade: every migrated site reads registry; bucket-c sites carry an explicit `[M-*]` marker, not a silent skip (§3). Regress: 0 delta vs clean binary, FULL `nova test` (sum-heavy: pattern matching, errors, Option/Result) — not a sample, because layout drift is silent.
- **Blast-radius:** Pattern matching, sum construction, equality/compare codegen for ALL sum types (Option/Result/user enums/errors). Measure: diff generated C for every fixture using `match` on a sum + every Option/Result test — must be byte-identical. This is the highest-risk U.6 task.
- **Deps:** U.6.2.a · **Risk:** High. Registry lookup precedence (Prelude>User>Baseline) could pick a different entry than legacy `sum_schemas` last-write-wins. De-risk: run in detect-mode first — at each migrated site, `debug_assert_eq!` legacy-result vs registry-result over a full corpus run; only switch the read after zero mismatches. Verify against CLEAN binary per §6.5.

> **РЕЗУЛЬТАТ U.6.2.b detect-measure + РЕОРГ §3 (2026-06-20).** Detect-прогон (non-fatal,
> release-бинарь с инструментацией field-layout сайтов + глобальный keyset-diff; sum-heavy
> корпус plan55/56/57/59/59_1/62/72/91/95/95bis/99/99_2_ctor/103_1/103_2/103_3/107/108/126/
> 131/133/134/136/138/153_3/162/163/generics/contracts/effects/narrowing) показал: **registry —
> НЕ верное зеркало legacy `sum_schemas`** по трём осям:
> - **A1 пустые sum'ы** (`RuntimeNoneError`, `Uninhabited`: emit_c.rs:10075/:10756 делают
>   `insert(HashMap::new())` БЕЗ `register_user_sum`) — legacy-only.
> - **A2 baseline-only**: `Option`/`Result`/`RuntimeError`/`NovaOpt_nova_int` есть в registry
>   ВСЕГДА из `init_hardcoded_baseline`; в legacy появляются только когда конкретный тест эмитит
>   их схему из `.nv` (per-test, не всегда).
> - **A4 erased-generic layout** (тихая, опасная): на `s32172` для `Result` legacy =
>   `.nv`-выведённое `{Ok:[Nova_T*], Err:[Nova_E*]}`, registry = baseline-хардкод
>   `{Ok:[nova_int], Err:[nova_str]}`. Остальные field-layout сайты (s12926/s19932/s30042) —
>   **0 дивергенций** на широком корпусе.
>
> **Вывод (направляющий §3, владелец 2026-06-20):** корень — **захардкоженные `variants` в
> `init_hardcoded_baseline`** (Option/Result/RuntimeError). Это тот «зашитый в компилятор» слой
